Yesterday, the Municipal Government issued a proclamation stating, "Based on the official letter from the Cotton Industry Control Committee of the National Economic Council and the Central Cotton Adulteration and Mixing Prohibition Office, it is stated that the director of the Shanghai Sub-Office, Tang Dongshan, reported that since the establishment of the office on October 16, it has been handling the registration of cotton merchants and the inspection of cotton in Dongjiapo, Zhoujiaqiao, Beixinjing, Donggou, Wusong, and other places. Most local cotton farmers and merchants have complied with the cotton merchant registration regulations and the prohibition regulations, as well as the inspection methods. However, some people have shown stubborn resistance and disregarded the law. If this continues without rectification, it will inevitably hinder the entire prohibition work. Therefore, it is proposed to request your office to send a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government to issue a notice, earnestly informing all cotton farmers and merchants to register in accordance with the regulations and submit to inspection, and to instruct the Public Security Bureau to order all sub-bureaus and police stations to do their best to assist in order to reduce resistance and facilitate progress. Based on this, it is found that the Jiangsu Provincial Districts and the Shanghai Municipal District Cotton Merchant Registration and Inspection Methods have been sent to your Municipal Government for promulgation and instructed the Public Security Bureau to effectively assist the sub-office in carrying out cotton merchant registration. In view of the previous situation, in addition to instructions, a corresponding letter is sent, hoping that you will review and issue several proclamations so that all cotton farmers and merchants will comply with the regulations for registration and await inspection by the sub-office. Also, please instruct the Public Security Bureau and its sub-bureaus to provide effective assistance at all times to facilitate implementation. Based on this, it is found that the cotton merchant registration methods and inspection methods in this municipal district have been promulgated by this government and the bureau has been instructed to assist. Now, based on the previous situation, in addition to issuing an order to the Public Security Bureau and replying by letter, a proclamation is jointly issued, instructing all cotton farmers and merchants in the city to register in accordance with the regulations and await inspection by the sub-office, and not to delay. Strictly enforce this proclamation."

Jiangsu Province National Goods Factories Association: This Year's Central Work is to Petition the Government to Lower Interest Rates to Reduce Burden and to Broadly Accept Inland Real Estate Mortgages as Collateral 107

Qian Chengxu, Director-General of the China Industrial Federation, attended the Jiangsu Provincial National Goods Factories Association cadre meeting in Changzhou a few days ago and has since returned to Shanghai. A reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency met with Mr. Qian at the association's Shanghai office yesterday morning, and he provided detailed information on the association's central work. The details are as follows:

Meeting Process

The Jiangsu Provincial National Goods Factories Association held a cadre meeting in Changzhou. More than ten people attended, including Hu Xiyuan, Xue Mingjian, Liu Guojun, Qian Chengxu, Liu Piji, Ding Zhixiang, Jiang Shangda, and Pan Guojun. Under the chairmanship of Xue Mingjian, it was resolved to revise the organizational charter, changing the director system to a committee system. Qian Chengxu, Xue Mingjian, Liu Piji, Ding Zhixiang, and Pan Guojun were appointed as standing committee members, forming a presidium to jointly assume external responsibilities. In addition, several important proposals, including the central work for this year, were decided upon.

Central Work

As for the association's central work for this year, it was decided that each member should be practically responsible and work hard, avoiding empty talk and striving for practicality. Starting from February 1st of this year, an investigation into the import of goods in various localities will be launched immediately. It is expected that this work will be completed within four months. The next step will be to statistically categorize the findings based on the nature and type of goods. If foreign goods are only slightly used, efforts will be made to design alternatives for factories or shops to replace them with national goods, gradually cultivating the public's love and use of national goods. In addition, more than ten letters have been sent to the relevant industry authorities of various countries, asking about the methods used in those countries to promote national goods, as a reference for our promotion of national goods.

Rescuing National Goods

The association, in view of the recent two years of increasing foreign goods flooding the inland, especially in the Su-Chang area, which has gradually become a center for foreign goods dumping due to convenient transportation, although there are many yarn and cloth factories in Changzhou, Wuxi, Suzhou, and other places, a large amount of foreign cotton cloth is still imported. In order to rescue the production and sales of national goods, this year has been designated as the "National Goods Year." The association is determined to fully support the development of national goods and adopt dumping methods to compete with foreign goods. The association has also submitted a petition to the provincial government, requesting the establishment of an industrial management committee within the Construction Bureau to be specifically responsible for maintaining industry.

Requesting Interest Reduction

Chinese factories face difficulties in competing with foreign goods due to excessive interest burdens and increased costs. For example, foreign-owned yarn factories in China borrow money from their domestic banks at interest rates of only 3.5% to 4%. Assuming that 20-count yarn is the standard, the interest burden per package of yarn is only three or four yuan. However, Chinese-owned yarn factories often pay interest rates of more than 1% per month for year-round loans. During the particularly urgent financial situation last year, the interest burden per package of yarn reached as high as sixteen or seventeen yuan. Although the government has already complied with the requests of the industrial sector and has clearly ordered interest rate reductions, there is still no definite method for reducing interest rates. Therefore, the association is submitting a petition requesting the government to promptly announce the method for reducing interest rates in order to benefit Jiangsu's industries.

Collateral Activities

The government's recently announced financial activities measures also include real estate mortgages as one of the ways to stimulate activity. However, the meaning of "real estate" primarily focuses on Shanghai real estate. As a result, Shanghai's land prices may increase, and cash from the interior will still flow into the city. Therefore, the focus of "real estate" should be inland real estate to avoid imbalances. The association is planning to submit a petition to the government, requesting that matters relating to real estate mortgages should start from inland real estate. In short, the difficulties currently experienced by industrial production in China are not limited to the above points, but they are urgently in need of resolution.

The total closing period for various industries in the 24th year of the Republic of China is approaching. Money shops are extending office hours and providing special flexibility for overdrafts for various industries, changing to term loans. Banks and money shops are busy collecting and settling accounts. Various industries hope that the Loan Committee will generously approve the credit loans that have been applied for. The details are as follows:

Special Flexibility: After the start of the total closing period for the 24th year, money shops will urge the return of overdrafts for various accounts, requiring them to be cleared before the 23rd and the deposit books returned. After the total closing, the money shops will distribute the deposit books. However, after the approval of the 18 million loan from the Central, China, and Communications Banks, the money shops are providing special flexibility to various accounts, allowing them to change the overdraft amount to term credit loans or term mortgage loans based on the creditworthiness of each account. The term is usually one or two months. These procedures are being handled these days.

Busy Collecting and Settling Accounts: With the total closing period approaching, banks and money shops have extended their office hours. The time is determined by each bank's and money shop's accounts. The money shops have decided to extend the ticket collection time to 5:00 PM starting from the 19th, and the ticket return time is extended by one hour compared to the past. Banks and money shops are very busy collecting and settling accounts. The money market's foreign exchange rate yesterday was still eight cents per thousand yuan per day. Money shops will be closed for four days from the 24th to sort everything out. Banks will be closed for three days from the 24th, called the Spring Holiday.

Your committee is in charge of the important task of loans, and you must have observed the situation. However, it is heard that there are still hundreds of loan applications from merchants that have been investigated and completed but have not been approved by the meeting. Furthermore, it is heard that there is no plan to convene a regular meeting to approve loans before the total closing period. The news has spread and the public is panicked. If this is true, thousands of merchants in the city may be forced to close down due to poor turnover, and the impact is worrying. It will not only create a major economic panic in the commercial market, but the society will also be shaken and uneasy. Our sub-branches are deeply concerned and dare to send this urgent telegram, requesting your committee to approve the various applications that have been investigated and completed, or are being investigated, as soon as possible before the total closing of the old calendar, and to release the loans immediately to relieve the urgent need and overcome the difficulties. We await your orders with urgency."

The association's purpose is related to the entire national mining industry, and the public's interests are at stake. Without presuming, we specially continue to express the sincerity of the companies. We respectfully believe that Your Excellency (arriving new) is wise and that coal is the mother of various industries, needed for national defense, and beneficial for the people's livelihood. With broad planning, you will immediately implement a protection policy. We respectfully request that you examine the original petitions of the companies and order (order the Ministry of Railways to implement) (consult the Ministry of Railways) to promptly revise the Pinghan Railway's coal and coke freight rates to be lighter and order the railway to implement them, so that the coal mines along the line can open up sales channels and celebrate their recovery. Hoping for good news, we cannot express our prayers enough."

Changshu Baimao Sluice Gate is Scheduled to Have a Groundbreaking Ceremony on the 30th of this Month; Fu Rulin Will Attend and Preside; Invitations are Extended to All Sectors to Participate in the Ceremony 118

The Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, in order to defend against the highest tide of the Yangtze River, is constructing the Baimao Sluice Gate in Dongzhang Town, Changshu County, and has scheduled a groundbreaking ceremony there at noon on the 30th of this month. Fu Rulin, Chairman of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, will attend and preside; invitations are extended to all sectors to participate in the ceremony. The details are as follows:

Gate Height

The height of the gate is based on the highest tide level of the Yangtze River (4.69 meters above the Wusong sea level zero point). The height of the gate sill is 1.5 meters below the Wusong sea level zero point. The gate has five openings, each 7.48 meters wide, and the gate body is 44 meters long. A bridge surface is erected on the gate to connect the automobile highway in the future. The entire gate is made of steel-reinforced concrete. The gate is a suspended type, using a counterweight to balance its weight, and is equipped with a lifting manual machine to control the opening and closing of the gate.

Ceremony Order

Ceremony Order: Meeting as usual, the Chairman delivers the opening remarks, the Commission reports on the Baimao Sluice Gate construction preparations, the National Economic Council delivers instructions, guest speeches, groundbreaking ceremony, cannons are fired, photography, ceremony concludes.

Transportation

Guests traveling from Nanjing will take the train to Wuxi, then transfer to the 7:00 AM car on the Hu-Xi Highway to Zhitang. Those traveling from Shanghai will take the 7:00 AM car on the Hu-Xi Highway. Those traveling from Suzhou will take the Su-Chang Road car to Changshu, then transfer to the Hu-Xi Highway car. The Commission will have a steamer in Zhitang to directly reach the work location, and will provide lunch at the Baimao Sluice Gate.

Postal and Telegraph Agencies on Two Railways; Suzhou and Other Stations Implemented Yesterday; Jiaxing and Other Stations on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Line Will Be Implemented Soon; All to Be Completed Before the 20th of This Month 119

According to Shen Shi News Agency, in order to facilitate passenger communication and closely link the entire state-run transportation business, the Ministry of Communications and Ministry of Railways created a postal and telegraph agency plan at railway stations across the country, and decided to pilot it at nine major stations on the two railways. Except for Shanghai North Station, which has been implemented since New Year's Day, Suzhou, Wuxi, and other stations also implemented it yesterday, accepting domestic and foreign language telegrams, urgent telegrams, and ordinary letters, registered letters, airmail letters, and express letters to Hong Kong, Macau, and other places from passengers. The Hangzhou and Jiaxing stations on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Line will be implemented soon. The entire plan is scheduled to be completed before the 20th. The postal and telegraph agency business hours are from 8:00 AM to 10:00 PM, but on Sundays and holidays, in addition to telegrams, all postal letters will be received and sent according to the post office's holiday hours. Passengers who want to send telegrams, letters, or use public telephones can contact the railway station postal and telegraph agency nearby at any time. If they want to send a telegram on the train, there are designated train service personnel from the railway bureau to assist them, which is very convenient.

Central, China, Communications, and Other Banks Provide Loans to Relieve the Market in Shandong Province; Total Loan Amount is 1 Million Yuan; Three Loan Methods Have Been Agreed Upon 120

Because the commerce of Shandong Province was affected by the economic downturn and was severely depressed, and the closing period for various industries has arrived, there is an urgent need for funds, the Shandong Provincial Department of Finance requested loans from the Central, China, Communications, and Minsheng Banks to provide relief. The loan amount will be 250,000 yuan each from the Central, China, Communications, and Minsheng Banks, totaling 1 million yuan. Representatives of Merchants and Citizens from Fourteen Counties in Henan Province Come to Shanghai to Petition for the Abolition of Oppressive Taxes on Huai Salt; After Petitioning the Salt Affairs Administration, They Will Go to Nanjing Again 121

The people of fourteen counties in the former Ruyang region of Henan Province, as well as Gushi, Huangchuan, Guangshan, Shangcheng, and Xixian counties, are all in the sales area for Huai salt. However, due to the heavy and miscellaneous taxes, merchants and citizens cannot bear the burden. Now that the border area between Henan and Anhui provinces has gradually been pacified, these oppressive taxes still exist in a disguised form. Therefore, merchants and citizens from fourteen counties have specially sent representatives, such as Zhou Longguang, to Shanghai yesterday, intending to petition the Salt Affairs Administration and then go to Nanjing again to petition the Ministry of Finance. The text of their petition is recorded as follows: "For the purpose of petitioning for the urgent implementation of the new salt law to relieve the disaster-stricken people and benefit the people's livelihood, the Huai salt transportation and sales Yinan, Ruguan and other fourteen counties, in addition to the unified tax at that time, did not have any additional taxes, which benefited both national planning and the people's livelihood. Since Mr. Zhao supervised Henan, taxes were first set up in Sanhejian, named salt increment price, followed by named food household donation, setting up cards to collect taxes, which was extremely oppressive. The people, under the power of lust, had no appeal. Fortunately, the Northern Expedition was completed, and the National Government, in the 19th year, issued a general order that salt increment was national revenue and should be uniformly collected by the Ministry of Finance. Local governments may not set up other names to collect additional taxes, and military and political leaders of all provinces should notify their subordinates that they must never establish any names under the salt increment project to collect additional taxes, etc. All our people are deeply grateful. Afterwards, the establishment of a sales supervision office in Sanhejian, Henan Province, was originally to compensate for the insufficiency of tax revenue, which was a temporary expedient, and then changed to a salt affairs tax bureau. However, the Huai salt is taxed at the place of origin in Haizhou, at a rate of four yuan per Zu. After Anhui Province adds one yuan and five corners, the Sanhejian Tax Bureau, only one river away, adds another one yuan and five corners, which is not equal treatment. In addition, according to the market scale, each load of salt is calculated at more than nine foreign yuan. Comparing the past and the present, the disparity is more than ten times. Moreover, the tax bureau sends teams to combat smuggling, harassing everywhere. Whenever they arrive at the market town, they are armed with guns, as if facing an enemy. The Gushi incident of killing civilians has not yet been resolved. The representatives humbly believe that the Sanhejian tax bureau is oppressing and harassing the people and is not conducive to national use. It really goes against the authorities' intention to reform the salt administration. Moreover, Gushi is located in the border area of ​​three provinces and has been ravaged by bandits and communists. In addition, there are floods and droughts, and the starving are full of the fields. The survivors of the catastrophe are waiting to be rescued. Regarding salt, how can we burden our people again? The representatives read in the newspaper that the Fifth Plenary Session of the Fifth National Congress proposed four cases for the implementation of the new salt law, which have been sent to the Resolutions Committee and should be considered for a comprehensive solution. For this reason, we request the urgent implementation of the new salt law and the elimination of the Sanhejian Tax Bureau, in order to relieve the disaster-stricken people and benefit the people's livelihood. We are afraid and await orders. Respectfully submitted to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance of the National Government."

Yuyao: Salt Merchant Representatives Remain in Shanghai to Petition 124

Around 11 a.m. the day before yesterday, salt merchant representatives Shang Cai Su and others continued to petition the General Office of Salt Affairs Inspection. They were received by Chief Inspector Feng. Details have already been reported in the press. The original petition is now transcribed below: It is submitted to request strict orders to be followed by wealthy merchants who are disobeying orders and delaying, to fully collect the quota in order to save the remaining breath of the salt farmers. Yuyao salt merchant Tu Tiren (also known as Shou Shan) manages the public granaries of the five districts, Gong Xing, Yuan Tai, and is coordinating a price reduction and suspension of collection in the granaries of eastern Zhejiang. Moreover, he has deceptively obtained approval from the Transportation Office to collect salt at a 60% rate. After repeated appeals from the representatives, the Ministry issued Order No. 1465 on December 14th of the 20th year of the Republic of China to the Salt Affairs Office of Liangzhe, instructing them to immediately respond by collecting the full quota and restoring the full collection of bundles to facilitate transportation and sales, without allowing any delays, etc. The Transportation Office also issued an order to the Yuyao field, which Field Director Zuo reiterated to promptly collect the full amount of salt and to ensure that the quota is collected in full within the year, without any delays, etc. Upon receiving this order, the granary merchant should immediately comply and fully collect the quota, so that the impoverished salt farmers struggling to survive at the end of the year can maintain their livelihoods. However, in January of this year, granary merchant Wang Shou Shan announced, "This granary, due to excessive production and sluggish sales, with difficult turnover, has had to temporarily suspend collection. Subsequently, we received an order from the Liangzhe Transportation Envoy Office instructing us to reduce the collection to 60% of the original quota from July of this year to provide relief. This granary, in order to uphold the government's policy and consider the people's livelihood, has repeatedly made efforts and reluctantly complied. Half a year has passed since the opening of collection. Currently, the sluggish sales show no hope, and financial exhaustion makes it difficult to maintain. However, because the end of the year is approaching and the livelihoods of the salt farmers are at stake, this granary, despite the great difficulties, will still try its best to comply with the order and collect the 60% quota first. We earnestly hope that all salt farmers will hand in their 60% quota and receive their salt money to safely pass the new year. As for restoring the remaining 40%, it is a separate matter. The granary merchant is also preparing to find another solution, considering all aspects and cooperating fully to resolve it as soon as possible. We hope you will not easily believe rumors, which will only cause more disputes and do no good, only increasing losses. Please pay attention," etc. His defiance of orders and refusal to immediately restore the full quota is simply aimed at taking advantage of the lunar new year to oppress the salt farmers beyond the already reduced price of eight jiao, reducing it even further. The intention is clear. The order from the Ministry is to fully collect the quota and restore the full collection of bundles. The field order also stipulates that the so-called restoration of the full quota within the year means continuing the full quota of the 24th year of the Republic of China without any doubt. However, the merchant's announcement says it is another matter and that he is preparing to find another solution, his tactics of delaying becoming increasingly sophisticated. The salt farmers, with their food and clothing almost exhausted, are in dire straits, and the situation is extremely dangerous and difficult to suppress. The representatives have exhausted their voices and efforts, unable to persuade them. Therefore, they have rushed to your office again, unable to prepare a written report, and on the 7th of this month, they personally requested that the merchant be strictly ordered to comply with the previous order. A representative was assigned to receive them. Given that the Ministry's order has already been sent to the Transportation Office, we still beg you to strictly order the Yuyao field to supervise and urge the granary merchant to comply with the order and make up the full quota of the 24th year of the Republic of China to save the remaining breath of the salt farmers. We are extremely anxious and await your orders. Respectfully submitted to Zhu Yun, Director of the General Office of Salt Affairs Inspection and Director of the Salt Affairs Office.

Ministry of Military Affairs Tests Coal Gas Vehicles 134

The Ministry of Military Affairs believes that coal gas vehicles are extremely important for national defense transportation. Therefore, on the 13th of this month, the Transportation Corps conducted a coal gas vehicle test. The vehicles being tested were the Lihe Dauntless brand coal gas passenger car from the Hankou China Coal Gas Engine Factory, with a load capacity of one and a half tons; the Chevrolet brand coal gas truck from the Shanghai Zhongming Second Factory, with a load capacity of one and a half tons; and the General Motors brand coal gas truck from the China Coal Gas Vehicle Company, with a load capacity of three tons. The main tester was German consultant Roman, along with several people including Transportation Corps technicians Shen Yunshan and Peng Hao, and Ordnance Department technician Hu Zongpu. On the 13th, the vehicles' mechanical components and load capacities were inspected in Nanjing. On the morning of the 14th, they departed from Nanjing for Shanghai. The weather was a mix of rain and snow, resulting in poor road conditions and strong winds. As a result, the China vehicle performed the best, arriving in Shanghai at 9 p.m. that day without any malfunctions along the way. The China Lihe vehicle broke down in Changshu at 12 p.m. the following morning due to a coal gas malfunction, so it switched to gasoline to drive to Shanghai. The Zhongming vehicle also broke down, arriving at 2 p.m. the following afternoon. It also switched to gasoline in Yixing due to a coal gas malfunction. It is reported that the China and Zhongming vehicles, after being repaired, will still travel from Shanghai to Nanjing via Hangzhou in the near future for another decisive test.

Rickshaw Puller Suspected of Collusion in Robbery by Taking Small Roads 138

Chen Longheng, a 30-year-old man from Ningbo, works for an oil company and lives at No. 8 Pude Lane, Menghua Street. Yesterday morning at 6 a.m., he arrived in Shanghai from Ningbo on the new Beijing steamship. At the pier, he hired a rickshaw pulled by Qi Youshan from Yancheng to go home. The rickshaw puller did not go west on Tongming Avenue but took small roads, circling around to the vicinity of Jingye Lane, Jukui Street, inside the Little East Gate. Suddenly, a bandit grabbed a呢帽 hat worth over ten yuan from Chen's head from behind the rickshaw and fled. Chen ordered Qi to stop the rickshaw, intending to chase after the bandit, but Qi pretended not to know and ran away. Chen jumped off the rickshaw and reported the incident to policeman Liu Wenhan, accusing the rickshaw puller, Qi Youshan, of being in collusion with the bandit. Verdict Reached in Bai Hongxun's Appeal Case 139

Lawyer Bai Hongxun from Zhenjiang, in the autumn of the year before last, colluded with a fugitive from Guangdong named Xu to falsely claim to be contracting the Western food service on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, and contacted Jiang Youtang from Ningbo and Feng Yishen from Tongzhou, agreeing to charge 33,000 yuan after the deal was completed. They first collected an opening fee of 1,800 yuan from Jiang and Feng, and Bai issued a receipt. Later, Jiang and others, seeing that the matter had not been completed for a long time, inquired at the Railway Bureau in the summer of last year, and learned that they had been deceived. The Railway Bureau reported the case to the judicial police for investigation and arrest. Xu had already fled, and only Bai Hongxun was arrested and sent to the Second Special Court. The Judicial Police Office filed a public prosecution on charges of fraud, and the two plaintiffs, Jiang and Feng, also hired lawyer Wu Peng to file an incidental private prosecution to recover the defrauded funds. After trial, Bai Hongxun was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment, fined 400 yuan, and ordered to compensate Jiang Youtang and Feng Yishen 1,800 yuan in foreign currency on June 17 of last year. Bai, dissatisfied with the verdict, filed an appeal with the Second Special Court Collegial Panel. The statement of reasons submitted was tens of thousands of words long, using over thirty sheets of paper. During the appeal period, Bai suffered from orchitis while in custody at the detention center, and his condition was critical. The presiding judge, after verifying the facts, entrusted his defense lawyers, Yu Hualong and Tang Hao, to be responsible for bailing him out for medical treatment. The case was temporarily suspended. Later, lawyers Yu and Tang learned that Bai, after being bailed out, had a plan to escape while receiving treatment in the hospital. They immediately applied to the court to withdraw the bail. The Second Special Court instructed the First Special Court to send police to the Shanghai Epidemic Hospital on Xizang Road on the 22nd of last month to arrest Bai. Permission was granted to find a suitable bail guarantor. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. Now, Bai's illness has healed. The Second Special Court's appellate court has concluded its investigation. Yesterday, Judge Wang Gangxu, along with judges Xiong 苹 and Sun Pengxian, and clerk Tao Zongkan, heard the case in the First Court Collegial Panel. Lawyer Fei Xizhen appeared in court on behalf of the Judicial Police Office. Appellant Bai Hongxun, accompanied by his defense lawyers Yu and Tang, appeared in court to state his reasons for appeal, mainly claiming that the matter was done by the fugitive Xu, and he was only acting as an intermediary. Although he received the money and issued a receipt, the money was given to Xu, etc. Subsequently, plaintiff Feng Yishen testified about the circumstances of the initial contact and payment. The court's inquiry and the lawyers' arguments lasted for three hours before the debate was declared closed, awaiting a scheduled sentencing. Bai was still released on the original bail.

Women's Temperance Union Asks Authorities to Eradicate Beggars in Shanghai; Plans to Form a Joint Beggar Eradication Association to Address Both Symptoms and Root Causes 140

Ms. Liu Wang Limin of the China Women's Temperance Union believes that the large number of beggars in Shanghai is a common sight, often begging on sidewalks, along streetcar stops, and at the entrances of alleys, not only obstructing traffic but also affecting the city's image. Therefore, she has drafted methods to address both the symptoms and root causes to eradicate beggars in Shanghai and has submitted a request to the municipal government for approval to instruct its subordinate departments to take action. The National News reporter has learned the details of the plan as follows: Establish a beggar registration office, funded by the Municipal Public Security Bureau in conjunction with the Public Concession and French Concession Public Works Departments. (Location) Borrowing public temples, ancestral halls, public stadiums, and churches would be most suitable. Force all beggars in the city to register at designated locations. Organize a joint beggar eradication association. The responsible groups are divided into three groups: (A) Child Beggar Relief Group, managed by the Child Welfare Association, Futong Shelter, and Longhua Orphanage; (B) Female Beggar Relief Group, managed by the Women's Relief Association, Shanghai Women and Children's Reformatory, and Rendesuo; (C) (Adult Male) Beggar Relief Group, managed by the Homeless Training Institute; Addressing the root cause, i.e., relieving beggars, is even more important. (D) Establish a Disabled Beggar Relief Group, managed by the School for the Blind and Deaf, Xinpuyu Hall, and Leprosy Relief Association; (E) Establish a Orphaned Beggar Committee, managed by Renjitang; Organize an Economic Committee. The administrative expenses will be jointly borne by the cooperating charitable organizations, but the educational and training expenses should be borne by the Beggar Relief Association. The fundraising methods are: (A) Beggars' lives today depend solely on the support of the middle class. Wealthy families always travel by car, and their doors are heavily guarded, so they are spared. Therefore, a property tax would be fair; (B) Mobilizing the Boy Scouts for fundraising and Western and Chinese charity sports competitions would be most effective; (C) Establish a charitable organization and a handicraft product sales outlet; (D) Establish a job placement department. These are the plans to eradicate beggars in Shanghai.

This City's Pawnbroking Industry Urges Reduction in Business License Fees; Social Affairs Bureau Orders Full Collection; Industry Claims Business is Declining, Requests 60% Reduction 141

The Pawnbrokers' Association of this city received an instruction from the Social Affairs Bureau stating that the period for the 20% reduction in business license fees for the industry had expired, and that full fees should be collected starting this year. The association, upon receiving the order, argued that the business of its members had been declining in recent years. It submitted a request to the bureau, asking them to forward it to the Municipal Government for approval to reduce the fees to 60% to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. The bureau's order and the association's submission are recorded below:

Social Affairs Bureau Order

Social Affairs Bureau Instruction No. 66, addressed to the Shanghai Pawnbrokers' Association: "Regarding the case of the 20% reduction in business license fees for pawnbroking shops in this city, as approved by the Municipal Government upon your bureau's submission in May of the 23rd year, with a two-year extension, and communicated by this bureau to all tax collection offices for compliance, the deadline for this reduction expires at the end of this year. Starting January 1st of the 25th year, full fees should be collected according to regulations to comply with the original plan. This order is issued to your bureau for your information, with the hope that you will immediately inform the pawnbroking industry association and all pawnbrokers not in the association." Dated January 15th of the 25th year of the Republic of China. Wu Xingya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau.

Pawnbrokers' Submission

Regarding the submission of a request: We received your bureau's Instruction No. 66 on January 15th (the order is quoted above). The member businesses of our association have suffered from market decline and sluggish business in recent years, making it difficult to sustain operations. Those declaring closure are increasing one after another, and those勉强勉强managing to stay open are also outwardly strong but inwardly weak, unable to see beyond the present. Regarding the aforementioned business license fees, they not only lack the ability to pay in full, but even the previous 20% reduction was difficult to bear. Therefore, our association, based on a resolution of the members on October 21st of last year, submitted a request to your bureau to forward it to the Shanghai Municipal Government, requesting that starting from the 25th year, the fees be reduced to 60% to show compassion. Now that the period for paying the license fees this year has arrived, the members are anxiously awaiting approval for pre-payment. However, upon receiving the forwarded order, they are inexplicably panicked. Given the dire straits of the industry, imposing additional burdens would be tantamount to a death sentence. Furthermore, the previous 20% reduction was originally intended to address the merchants' difficulties. As the situation has become even more difficult today, relying on precedent, we believe a re-approval is appropriate. Therefore, we continue to submit this request, earnestly hoping that your bureau will consider the merchants' plight, quickly forward the matter to the Shanghai Municipal Government, promptly approve the request, and also advise the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau to instruct all tax collection offices to temporarily suspend collection to provide relief and comfort those who are yearning for it, which would be greatly appreciated. Respectfully submitted to Wu, Director of the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau.

Minutes of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association Board Meeting: Investigation Decided on the Jiaxing Road Disturbance 142

The Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association convened its 26th board meeting on the 14th of this month at its new association hall, No. 288 Maigen Road. All directors attended except for Mr. Cang Gongwen and Mr. Qiu Zitong. Rickshaw puller director He Wushan sent a letter requesting leave, which was immediately approved, and alternate rickshaw puller director Zhu Fengxiang was temporarily appointed. Subsequently, the meeting discussed the conflict that occurred at the Jiaxing Road headquarters last Thursday. The general manager submitted a letter of report. After discussion, it was resolved:

The board of directors should express condolences to all injured staff members, and the board should extend special condolences to General Manager Zhang Dengying, who was attacked by thugs and seriously injured. Furthermore, it should be recorded that the board of directors is very satisfied with General Manager Zhang's service and firmly believes that Zhang's actions are all based on the welfare of all members of the mutual aid association and are perfectly in line with the guidelines set by the board of directors.

The board of directors should make every effort to investigate and bring the thugs to justice and subject them to legal sanction, and prevent similar incidents from happening in the future. In addition, it was learned that Zhang Dengying would soon recover and return to work. The board members were delighted to hear this, saying that Zhang's position was important and irreplaceable. Regarding the second resolution, a small committee was organized to handle the investigation and ensure that the real instigator is brought to justice. Moreover, what can be reported regarding this riot is that after the incident, rickshaw pullers who truly understood the matter were extremely indignant that some rickshaw pullers were being used. Three hundred and eighty-eight rickshaw pullers jointly sent a letter to the Rickshaw Committee expressing condolences for General Manager Zhang's injuries. The gist of the letter was that they feared Zhang would resign due to his injuries and that they would feel deeply regretful. They also stated that because of the hasty timing, only 388 people signed the letter, but the intention of the letter was truly the public opinion of the majority of rickshaw pullers.

Subsequently, the meeting discussed association affairs and the reports of various committees. The association affairs statistical report stated that the total number of medical diagnoses in December was 15,404, of which 2,569 were new cases. There were 691 relief cases, and nurses visited 637 districts. The December report of the Relief and Special Assistance Committee was approved. Among them, a certain charitable organization in Zhabei requested relief, but it was decided that the scope of the mutual aid association's relief was limited to rickshaw puller members, so it could not be approved. The minutes of the Insurance Committee meeting on December 27 were approved. The personnel committee of the labor service center convened a meeting on December 30 and, in principle, approved the Medical Committee's suggestion to use the upper floor of the Maigen Road association hall to establish a small hospital. However, the establishment of a coffin workshop was not approved because the measure was extremely uneconomical and it would be better to establish appropriate terms with outside coffin shops to have them handle it. The board of directors decided to organize a small committee to continue investigating the matter and also investigate matters such as coffin transport and public cemeteries. In addition, it was decided to seek entertainment for rickshaw pullers during the upcoming Spring Festival, and the location should be as widespread as possible. Later, the records of the Medical Committee were discussed. Regarding the establishment of a small hospital on the upper floor of the Maigen Road association hall, in addition to some regulations on the opening and operating costs, the original proposal was approved.

It is afraid of fire and does not dare to approach it. Habitat: Europe and Asia. Uses: For research, and its fur is used to make fur coats.

Japanese Residents Are Increasingly Impoverished; Unable to Repay Loans from the Japanese Government 144

According to the Japanese-language "Japanese Daily News," since the Shanghai Incident, Japanese residents have suffered great losses. The Japanese government, through the Consulate General, lent 5.3 million yuan of reconstruction funds to the Japanese Residents' Association. The loan agreement stated that the funds would be repaid to the government over ten years, starting in the Showa 13th year (Republic of China 27th year). However, the Japanese residents in this city who received these reconstruction funds have been operating since the incident, and their financial situation has become increasingly depressed. Furthermore, due to anti-Japanese sentiment, all Japanese residents have suffered a great blow. Therefore, those who manage to rebuild their businesses with the loans, regardless of the amount of capital borrowed, suffer equally. They have been forced to request the Japanese government to extend the repayment period stipulated in the loan agreement to thirty years. At 2:00 PM on the 15th, Japanese representatives Mr. Lin, Mr. Sakai, Mr. Ota, Mr. Kimura, and Mr. Takematsu discussed the matter at the Japanese Club. They all agreed that the Japanese residents in this city had suffered great losses due to the Shanghai Incident, and since then, the business and industrial sectors have been in a state of recession. Therefore, they requested the government to extend the ten-year repayment period stipulated in the loan agreement, starting in the year after next, to thirty years. However, applying to the government solely on behalf of Shanghai is unlikely to be effective. They plan to take the same steps in Tianjin and Qingdao. A concrete meeting is scheduled for the 19th to request assistance from government officials and businessmen.

Yin Gendao Has Evil Intentions: Commits Theft and Arson; Uses the Money to Buy New Clothes; Confesses to the Crime and Is Sentenced to Three and a Half Years 145

A certain Gu A'gen from Pudong opened a tin shop at No. 158 Xinji Beach Road. He had a younger brother named Gendao (22 years old), who was naturally unruly and specialized in wandering around. Recently, his sister-in-law returned to her hometown in Pudong for her grandmother's funeral. Unexpectedly, Gendao developed malicious intentions. At 6:00 PM on the 4th of this month, he bought a bottle of kerosene from a nearby store for thirty copper coins. At midnight, he sneaked into his brother's bedroom, opened the box, and stole two gold rings, a gold lock pendant, seventy yuan in paper money, and three silver dollars, worth a total of one hundred and forty-one yuan. He took them out and hid them in a trash can in the alley. At about 1:00 AM, he poured the kerosene on the firewood and set fire to two places:

In his brother's bedroom;

Beside the stove by the wind furnace in the kitchen.

After setting the fire, he fled to the road, 静ly trying to burn the house down and destroy the evidence. Fortunately, apprentice Yin Hanzhong and carpenter Shi Genfu, who was procrastinating at A'gen's place, noticed and managed to extinguish the fire. Gendao returned at about 2:00 AM and pretended not to know about the fire. Later, Hua Police No. 1344 arrived after being alerted and, after investigating, took Gendao to the police station. Under questioning by the police chief, he denied it and, without evidence, was released. The day before yesterday, Yin A'gen returned to the shop and found that the banknotes and ornaments in the box were missing. He knew what his brother had done. However, after getting the money, he sold the gold rings and other items to silver shops, bought a whole new set of clothes, including a wool coat, leather robe, shoes, a watch, and a leather wallet, and indulged himself in various entertainment venues. At about 7:00 PM that evening, A'gen found him at the Yong'an Rooftop Garden, twisted him over to Hua detective Sun Shaokun, who arrested him and placed him in the Huishan police station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. 工部局 Lawyer Zhang Shizhu detailed the previous circumstances and asked for an investigation. Yin A'gen, Yin Hanzhong, and Shi Genfu testified about what happened. Detective Sun presented a leather wallet, containing twenty yuan in paper money and a watch, which had been confiscated from the defendant. Questioned, the defendant's testimony was evasive, and he pleaded for leniency. Judge Jiang Shuzi sentenced Yin Gendao to three years and six months of imprisonment, and ordered the leather wallet, banknotes, and watch to be returned to Yin A'gen.

A Scandal Arises from Taking a Concubine; An Elderly Man Attempts Suicide; His Face Turns White and He Staggers; Sent to Hospital for Treatment, His Life Can Be Saved 146

Zhu Jinfu, a Cantonese man over fifty years old, has been working as a clerk at the Jianghai Customs for more than ten years. He is from a modestly prosperous family and currently lives at No. 35 Wenhua Lane, Shigao Tower Road, Hongkou. Zhu's wife, Deng, is middle-aged. The couple has always been very harmonious. Unexpectedly, Zhu's attitude has changed this year. He likes to patronize prostitutes and has become inextricably linked to a Cantonese prostitute named Li Yuejuan. Li is in her early twenties and has a beautiful appearance, so Zhu loves her more than anything. Li also benefits from his wealth and serves him attentively. As a result, Zhu is completely besotted and, fearing that the good times will not last, plans for the long term. He spent a thousand yuan to exclusively hire Yuejuan and rented a room for her at No. 19 Delin Apartment, Chongming Road, as a golden house. The two live together like husband and wife. Zhu's wife, Deng, has heard rumors but has not known the location of his hidden mistress, so she has had to endure it for the time being. Recently, Zhu felt that it was inconvenient to keep Yuejuan in an external residence for a long time, so he made further plans to redeem Yuejuan's freedom and return her to live with his wife. He discussed it with the madam, and an agreement was reached. Yesterday, he discussed it with his wife, but Deng not only refused but also flew into a rage. Zhu feared that Yuejuan would hear about it and ruin the good thing, so he burst into tears of regret. He harbored resentment and, taking advantage of a moment when no one was paying attention, secretly swallowed sleeping pills, hoping to die for love. Later, remembering that he would not see his beloved again, he went to Delin Apartment. When the two met, they told each other the whole story and cried in each other's arms. At that moment, Li Yuejuan suddenly saw that Zhu's face had turned white, his breathing was rapid, and he was about to fall. She was shocked and, after repeated questioning, he revealed the truth. Li Yuejuan was terrified upon hearing this. She quickly reported to the police station, which dispatched a car to send him to Tongren Hospital for treatment, only saying that Zhu was suffering from a stroke, unaware of the hidden story. It is reported that the poisoning was not severe and his life is expected to be saved.

Two Unjust Deaths: Wu Yousheng Hangs Himself Due to Financial Difficulties; Zhang Linfu Commits Suicide After Being Scolded by His Father 148

Wu Yousheng, a native of Jiangyin, 39 years old, lived at No. 7 Doupai, Jinsheng Lane, Jinsheng Road. He used to work as a packer in Shandong. Last August, he was dismissed for some reason and came to Shanghai, but he was still unemployed. His wife, Xu, currently works at the Shenxin Yarn Factory. However, her income is very small, making it impossible to support a family of several people. Therefore, the economic situation was extremely strained. Wu, after thinking about it the day before yesterday, was resentful and despondent. That night, while his wife and children were asleep, he hanged himself on an iron pole in the room. At about 4:00 AM yesterday morning, his wife discovered him and hurriedly tried to get him down, but he was already barely breathing. She reported the matter to the Yulin Road Police Station, which dispatched detectives to investigate and summoned an ambulance to the scene. Wu was rushed to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective and he soon died. In addition, Zhang Linfu, a local man, just turned twenty, lived at No. 8 Yifeng Lane, Guizhou Road. His father, Zhang Songren, currently works as a bookkeeper at the Tianran Hotel. The day before yesterday, a jacket suddenly went missing at home. Suspecting that his son had stolen it, he scolded Linfu severely. However, that afternoon, Linfu, after being scolded, felt extremely resentful and despondent and committed suicide by secretly swallowing opium smoke. His mother discovered him groaning in bed and rushed him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective and he soon died. The hospital reported the matter to the Lao Zha Police Station, which ordered detectives to investigate. The bodies of the two men were sent to the forensic examination office on Filun Road by the respective police stations. Yesterday morning, Zhang Zongru, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, accompanied by forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the office and confirmed that the deaths were indeed suicides. They instructed the family members to separately sign statements and take the bodies back for burial.

The Ancient Vase Case Has Just Concluded; Now There's a Diamond Ring Lawsuit; Cheng Linsheng Sues Jiang Zhaoting for Fraud; Jiang Files a False Accusation Against Cheng for Debt 149

Jiang Yuting, a Wuxi native and owner of the Yuanzhang Gold and Silver Jewelry Store at No. 99 Shanxi Road, was previously sued by Chi Yunfei for defrauding him of a Guyuexuan ancient vase. The First Special District Court sentenced Jiang to eight months of imprisonment, but the sentence was suspended. Now, Jiang has been sued by real estate tycoon Cheng Linsheng, represented by lawyer Hu Jue, in the First Special District Court for fraud and breach of trust. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Jiang Shuzi opened the Second Criminal Court for interrogation. Cheng Linsheng did not attend. Lawyer Hu stated the reasons for the prosecution, saying, in brief, that the plaintiff had two diamond rings, one worth 10,000 yuan and one worth 4,000 yuan. In the second month of the lunar calendar last year, the defendant said that someone wanted to buy one of the rings and wanted to take it to view it. At that time, the plaintiff handed the ring over to him, but he never returned it. On November 3rd, he suddenly sent a letter through a lawyer, saying that the ring had been used as collateral for Cheng's debt of 18,000 yuan. In this situation, he committed the crimes of fraud and breach of trust under Articles 339 and 342 of the Criminal Code. He requested that the court issue a judgment according to the law. Cheng Linsheng went to Nanjing for business today and could not attend court. Questioned, Jiang Yuting said that Cheng owed me 18,000 yuan for goods and issued three checks, which were all returned due to insufficient funds. Cheng then handed over the two diamond rings for me to sell, and the proceeds were used to repay the debt. However, the two rings were only worth 6,000 yuan and had no buyer. Cheng then said that they would be used as collateral. Because their value was less than 18,000 yuan, he also used the Guyuexuan vase as collateral. He then colluded with Chi Yunfei to sue me for fraud and is now suing me again. Therefore, I am filing a false accusation counterclaim. He hired lawyers Lu Shaozong and Yu Zhonglu to defend him and said that he had already filed a lawsuit to redeem the collateral against Cheng. He then presented the checks and lawsuits to the court. Judge Jiang found the facts clear and ordered the closing arguments, then announced the end of the trial and scheduled the verdict for next Tuesday.

Gao Er Branch Director Xu Weizhen Yesterday Held Inauguration Ceremony; Judicial Administration Department Sends Liang Renjie to Supervise; Xue Dubi and Others Delivered Speeches 150

After Xu Weizhen, Director of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, came to Shanghai at the end of last year to take over the affairs, he held an inauguration ceremony at the Gao Er Branch on Zhejiang Road at ten o'clock yesterday morning. Liang Renjie, Director of the Gao San Branch, was sent by the Judicial Administration Department to supervise the oath. More than a hundred representatives from all walks of life in the party, government, industry, and commerce attended. A record of the grand occasion is as follows:

Representatives from All Walks of Life Attending the Ceremony: The representatives from all walks of life in the party, government, industry, and commerce who attended included Liang Renjie, Director of the Gao San Branch and Supervisor representing the Judicial Administration Department; Luo Panhui, representing Mayor Wu of the Municipal Government; Jiang Huaisu, representing the Municipal Party Headquarters; Deng Peiyi, representing the Municipal Security Office; Chen Qiaozuo, representing the Garrison Headquarters; Jiang Hechun, representing the Finance Bureau; Ye Zhendong, County Magistrate of Shanghai County; He Dekui of the 工部局; Chen Tingrui, representing the Shanghai Lawyers Association; Luo Tong, Director of the Local Court; Zhou Jue, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Zhao Tiezhang, Deputy Director; and more than a hundred people including Xue Dubi, Xu Xiuzhi, Ye Zhuotang, Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, Xu Peihuang, Zhao Jinqing, and Wang Yunwu.

Xu Takes Oath, Liang Delivers Instructions: At precisely ten o'clock, Xu Weizhen, under the supervision of Liang Renjie, Supervisor representing the Judicial Administration Department, began the inauguration ceremony. After performing the ritual, Xu Weizhen read the oath, saying: "I solemnly swear that I will respectfully abide by the late Premier's will, obey the Party's principles, abide by the laws, be loyal to my duties, not waste a single penny, not misuse a single person, and never engage in embezzlement, bribery, or anything that violates this oath. I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This is my oath." After the oath, Liang Renjie, Supervisor from the Ministry of Justice, delivered instructions, saying in brief: "The purpose of law in the country is to balance human rights. Shanghai is the hub of national politics, economy, and culture. The manifestation of the spirit of the legal system must not be neglected in such a large city. Director Xu served in the temporary court in Shanghai in the 16th year and was later transferred. During the One-Two-Eight Incident, he served as the Director of the Gao Er Branch. This is his third time. The situation in Shanghai is well understood by Director Xu and he is always able to handle it with ease. I hope that after taking office, he will abide by the orders of the Ministry of Justice and the spirit of the law to serve the country and the people."

Xu Weizhen (Photo by Guan Zhen)

Representatives Delivered Speeches: Jiang Huaisu, representing the Municipal Party Headquarters, then delivered a speech, saying: "The social situation in Shanghai is extremely complex. All evil forces and reactionary forces are hidden within it. Only capable individuals can take on this responsibility. Director Xu has served in the judicial circles of Shanghai for many years. Today, he is returning to the old place and should be able to understand the past and innovate for the future. Today, on the occasion of Director Xu's inauguration, I have a few words to offer as a humble contribution: Those engaged in the judicial field must not only be able to 'endure labor,' but also be able to 'bear grievances.' They must not only 'avoid injustice,' but also 'avoid indulgence.' In handling judicial cases, I hope that they will take into account not only national law, but also natural justice and human sentiment." Xue Dubi then delivered a speech, saying: "Director Xu's return to the Gao Er Branch is truly a deep recognition of talent. In this period of frequent foreign invasions and serious national crisis, what we perceive is that only military affairs and diplomacy can save the country from ruin. We do not know that in addition to this, the judiciary also bears the heavy responsibility of national revival. History has the example of King Goujian of Yue, who spent ten years gathering strength and ten years teaching, and was able to avenge Wu. All of these are ancient lessons that the world can be won and saved by winning the hearts of the people through law. Therefore, to resolve the current national difficulties, we must engage in both internal stability and external resistance. External resistance requires concentrating the strength of the whole country to unite against the outside. Internal stability requires unifying the legal system to consolidate the national foundation. However, the Chinese people are still far from the concept of the legal system. For example, in Shanghai, the unrest of all evil forces truly makes those engaged in the judicial field feel disheartened. But we must not be discouraged because of this. We should uphold the law like a mountain and make the people abide by the law. Then the declining morale of the Chinese people can be reversed, and the crisis of national survival can be saved. Director Xu is returning to this court, and we are willing to uphold the spirit of serving the judicial field in the past and shoulder this responsibility." Finally, Wang Yunwu, Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, He Dekui, and others also delivered speeches. The speeches were too long to be recorded.

Xu Responds and Thanks for Encouragement: Finally, Xu Weizhen delivered a response, saying in brief: "I have been ordered to serve in the judicial circles of Shanghai for the fourth time. The first time I served in the temporary court without holding an inauguration ceremony. The second time I served as the Director of the temporary court and the Director of the Appeals Court. The third decision to serve as the Director of the Gao Er Branch was the same as today's fourth decision, holding an inauguration ceremony. Today, many of the representatives from the party, government, and other agencies who have attended previous times are here again today. I have not dared to forget the words of encouragement from the past several years. Today, I have received instructions and encouraging words from Director Liang of the Judicial Administration Department, Committee Member Jiang of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and all of you. I will not dare to fail to work diligently and follow them, serving the country and the people, in order to live up to your expectations." After the ceremony, a group photo was taken. Xu also told a New Voice News Agency reporter after the ceremony that he would not change a single one of the internal staff of the Gao Er Branch after taking office in order to streamline the process and achieve efficiency in the work. The current record officer is Zhang Dabing.

Lawsuit Involving Ballad Singers: Dispute Arising from the "Yang Guifei" Ballad Story; Shen Jian'an and Others Sue Wu Jianqing for Insult 153

Shen Jian'an and Xue Xiaoqing, ballad singers from the Guangyu Society in Wumen, recently hired lawyer Chen Yun to file a complaint with the First Special Court, accusing Wu Jianqing of public defamation in violation of Article 310 of the Criminal Code, and requesting compensation for damages of one yuan in national currency. The essence of their lawsuit is as follows: The plaintiffs have been performing ballads in Shanghai for many years. Last spring, they compiled a ballad story based on the history of the Tang Tianbao era, titled "Yang Guifei." After completing a portion of it, they intended to broadcast it every night on the Guohua Radio Station starting on October 1st. The defendant, Wu Jianqing, upon hearing this news, personally visited Shen Jian'an and offered to revise the ballad script. The plaintiffs, believing that the defendant had considerable expertise in the opening verses of ballads, agreed. After providing him with a portion of the draft, the two parties could not agree on the amount of remuneration, so the matter was dropped. Unexpectedly, the defendant harbored resentment and published a series of insults in the Xin Xin Chunqiu newspaper. He also placed large advertisements, claiming that the plaintiffs' "Yang Guifei" was a plagiarism of his "Biography of Yu Huan," which they had disguised and were broadcasting privately. He also complained to Huang Zhaolin, the president of the Guangyu Society, and Wei Yuqing, Xue Xiaoqing's teacher, deliberately damaging their reputation. Therefore, they filed this lawsuit. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang Qianchang of the Ninth Criminal Court summoned the plaintiffs, Shen Jian'an and Xue Xiaoqing, along with lawyer Chen, to court. They also submitted the script as evidence. The defendant, Wu Jianqing, did not appear but sent a lawyer, who stated that Wu was unable to attend due to illness and requested a postponement. He also filed a counterclaim. Judge Yang ordered that the case be rescheduled for a hearing in seven days.

Former Maid Sues for Moral Offense 158

Wang Xueyao, son of Wang Wanao, owner of the Wangji rickshaw company at No. 135 Avenue Heny, French Concession, is known as Wang Xiaokai. He is nearly thirty years old and has a wife and children. Recently, Chen Gaomin (29 years old), a former maid from Yangzhou, hired lawyer Li Ming to file a lawsuit with the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court, accusing him of moral offense, inciting abortion, and abandoning his wife. According to the complaint, on the night of June 29th of last year, after the plaintiff took a bath and went to sleep, the defendant Wang Xueyao pried open the door in the middle of the night and entered the room. He raped her and continued to rape her several times, causing her to become pregnant. Wang ordered her to have an abortion, but she refused because she was afraid of endangering her life. He then designed to dismiss her and abandoned her. She returned to her hometown and was driven out by her husband. Unable to make a living, she came to Shanghai to find Wang, but he refused to see her. In desperation, she filed a lawsuit requesting a trial. The court summoned him once on the 31st of last month, but the defendant was unable to appear because he was in his hometown. The date was changed. Yesterday, Judge Li Changnian held a hearing, summoning the defendant Wang Xueyao and his lawyer, Jin Zhi, to court. The plaintiff first testified about the rape and pregnancy. When asked, the defendant said that the accusation of rape was false and requested that the plaintiff be ordered to compensate him for his loss of reputation. The court examined the statements and ordered that the case be adjourned for further investigation.

Rickshaw Puller Commits Theft Due to Unemployment 159

On the morning of the 14th of this month, four robbers armed with guns suddenly arrived at the residence of a card player at No. 426 Avenue Joffre, French Concession. They robbed him of more than one hundred yuan in cash and fled. The victim chased after them and called the police. Inspector Tang Yunqing, detectives Qian Yumin, Wu Lianrong, and Sun Xueqin of the French Concession Police Station intercepted one of the robbers, Liu Wanlin, and took him into custody. This was briefly reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the victim is a local woman, Zhang Bin. When the detective arrested Liu, they found the original stolen money, one hundred and sixty yuan, intact on his person. Yesterday morning, the police station escorted Liu to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. Lawyer Chen Ming of the Police Department presented the case and requested a postponement to arrest the other accomplices and investigate before filing a lawsuit. The detective then reported the arrest process and presented the stolen money to the court. The victim, Zhang Bin, also came to court and described the robbery, saying that the robbers knew how to make water from a tap at home. Pretending that it was damaged, the fake company came and broke in. Liu confessed that he was eighteen years old, was from Yancheng, used to drive a rickshaw, is now unemployed, and has no home. Yesterday, he was invited by Father Chen and Wang Sanye, who are at large, to go to rob. He doesn't know where they are hiding now. Judge Li Changnian examined the statement and ordered that the case be adjourned to the 22nd for another trial. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Wang Jianfan and Others Sued for Property Division 161

Lawyer Wang Jianfan is originally from Dinghai, Zhejiang. His father, Zhongkun, had five sons and one daughter. Jianfan is the eldest, followed by Jianxun, Jianyan, Jianji, and Jianwu. Zhongkun owned property in Shanghai in Houshengli, Zhaofeng Road, and jointly opened the Shenda Soy Sauce Garden with others on Tangshan Road. In his hometown, he owned 180 mu of land, so his family was quite wealthy. Jianfan's younger brothers are still receiving higher education. Zhongkun passed away in the fourth year of the Republic of China, and the family affairs were managed by Jianfan's mother. In the 21st year, the mother also passed away. Jianfan, as the eldest brother, took on the responsibility of managing the family. His fourth brother, Jianji, married Hu Yinghua and had two children, Ruchang and Ruli. The elder one is only five years old, and the younger one is only two years old. Jianji died of illness in July of the previous year. Now his wife, Hu Yinghua, is requesting a division of the ancestral property. Zhongqing, her uncle, had originally mediated a settlement, but Jianfan and others reneged. Therefore, Hu hired lawyer E Sen to file a lawsuit with the First Special District Court against Wang Jianfan and his four brothers, requesting a division of the property. The lawsuit claims that the Shenda Soy Sauce Garden has six shares in total, which should be divided into five parts. Jianji's children should receive one share and two-fifths. There are twelve buildings in Houshengli, Zhaofeng Road. The other five brothers have already received two buildings each, leaving two buildings, which should be divided into five parts. There are also 180 mu of land in Dinghai, which should be divided into 30 mu. In addition, there is the income from the rent of the two buildings since August of the 21st year, which should be divided into 303 yuan. The income from the land rent should be divided into 576 yuan. She requests that the court make a judgment according to law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Tao held a hearing. First, lawyer E stated the purpose of the lawsuit. Then, Wang Jianfan replied that he admitted that the amount of Shenda shares and the ancestral land that the plaintiff should receive was true. As for the twelve buildings on Zhaofeng Road, they had been divided into six parts in the 19th year according to their mother's instructions, with each of the five brothers and their sister receiving two buildings each. He said that the house that the plaintiff was arguing about had long been rented out to his sister, and he produced the account book, saying that the income from the land rent and the soy sauce garden had also been divided equally according to the shares. The court ruled that it was necessary to investigate the evidence further and ordered that the case be adjourned for another trial.

Correspondence 169

To whom it may concern:

We have received a statement from Yuan Linjiang, claiming that he read a news item in the Shenmin and other newspapers on the 14th of this month, titled "Manure Boat Capsizes at Chenjiazhui," which stated, "As the ferry routinely sounded its horn before leaving, the sailboat suddenly veered to the left, crossing the bow of the ferry. The ferry immediately stopped its engines and reversed." This account is inconsistent with the facts. Mr. Yuan states that on the 13th of this month, at approximately 11:00 AM, his sailboat, Shanghai Registration No. 694, was sailing northeast in the Huangpu River near the Qujiang Wharf when it was struck from behind and the stern destroyed by Municipal Ferry No. 3, causing it to sink. After the accident, the ferry did not stop until passengers on board intervened. Four workers and passengers were rescued, including a passenger named Changsheng, who died from his injuries after being rescued. The worker Yuan Xiangjiang is still missing, presumed drowned. Mr. Yuan has commissioned your esteemed law firm to write to the Shenmin and other newspapers, requesting a correction of the facts. Therefore, we request that you investigate and correct the matter, for the sake of public interest. Respectfully submitted to the Shenbao Newspaper Office, Attorney Li Zonghong, January 16th.

A Visit to the China Electric Light Bulb Factory 170

— Huang Jiping

In recent years, the domestic electrical appliance industry has shown signs of vigorous growth. Although the nascent electrical industry is under pressure from foreign businesses, several of our electrical experts are still working diligently to manufacture and compete in the market. They are not deterred by the current difficulties. On the other hand, the desire among Chinese people to purchase domestic goods has become widespread and resolute. These two trends are indeed signs of the development of domestic industry. The scope of the electrical appliance industry is vast, including motors, fans, light bulbs, welding equipment, electrical wires, etc. Among these, light bulbs are something that most people living in cities consider indispensable. Therefore, the market for light bulbs is broader than that of other electrical appliances. A little over ten years ago, China did not have any factories manufacturing light bulbs, and those who needed them could only rely on foreign products. Now, we can use "Apollo" or "China" light bulbs, both of which are truly domestic products. It is said that there are now six or seven or more factories manufacturing light bulbs, with brands such as Huatong, Yongming, Fulaisheng, Yongliang, Xinguanghua, Guohua, Guotai, Zhonghua, Zhongguo, Desiling, Yaerden, Mingguang, Haoyou, and Daguangming. Among these, "Apollo" and "China" are the two largest factories, and their products are also more popular. This newspaper published an article about Apollo a month ago. Here, I would like to introduce the general situation of "China" to the readers:

The day before yesterday, at 3:00 PM, the sky was overcast, and the weather was rather gloomy. At the invitation of the owner of China Electric Light Bulb Factory, I went to visit. Our party of four, including Huang Zijian, Ye Changlie, Wu Jinfang, and myself, took a car to the new China factory on Ouyang Road. The General Manager, Tang Zhaoneng, the Manager and Engineer, Li Qingxiang, and the Deputy Engineer, Li Qinghua, had been waiting for us for some time. After chatting over tea for a while, we learned that China Electric Light Bulb Factory has only been around for seven years. Initially, it was capitalized with 50,000 yuan, and the factory was located on Xi'an Road in Hongkou, specializing in the production of both thermos bottles and electric lights. Later, it focused solely on light bulbs. It moved to the new factory last November. The factory building is not large, but the structure is very sophisticated. The scale is not large, but the equipment is very modern. It is truly an economical and rational factory. It currently has over fifty employees and one hundred and eighty workers, producing 5,700 light bulbs per day, with monthly sales of approximately 40,000 yuan. The products include Silver Light Bulbs (Argon), Haole Bulbs (Vacuum), Long Filament Bulbs (Vacuum), Argon Bulbs (i.e., Half Bulbs), White Milk Bulbs (Argon), Sky Blue Bulbs (Argon), Haole Bulbs (Vacuum), Showcase Light Bulbs, Natural Multi-Colored Bulbs, etc., ranging from 3 watts to 2,000 watts, all varieties available. The largest sales are in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, followed by Hunan, Anhui, and Guangdong. Many orders are placed from all over the country. They adhere to the principle of selling existing stock and rarely have any inventory left over. They have over 700 electrical supply stores acting as distributors, so they do not worry about sales channels. Road lights in various provinces and cities, railways, trams, ships, government agencies, and companies all place orders. Therefore, the business is becoming more and more prosperous.

After our initial conversation, we were led by the Chief Engineer and toured the factory, following the order of manufacturing: the glass bulb department, the mixing department, the wire-drawing department, the filament winding department, the filament inspection department, the filament mounting department, the core assembly department, the sealing department, the vacuum pumping department, the gas filling department, the light inspection department, the life testing department, the copper cap mounting department, the light testing department, the packaging department, and the storage department. It took us two hours to carefully examine everything. A small light bulb, from glass sand to finished product, involves forty-seven different procedures. This shows that the creation of every object, whether by machine or by hand, is not an easy task. We felt that two points were particularly praiseworthy during our visit: First, Chief Engineer Li spent two years developing the Silver Light Bulb, which uses silver converted into liquid to coat the inner layer of the bulb, producing a unique light. Its function is equivalent to a light bulb with a reflector, but with the added benefits of energy saving, brightness, and aesthetics. This is his new invention, and the Ministry of Industry has granted him a five-year patent. It is still rarely used in the market, and most people probably do not know about it. Second, after China Light Bulbs became popular, foreign brands such as General Electric, Osram, and Philips suffered a major setback. Therefore, they formed an alliance to compete with China, creating a very intense situation. Fortunately, China's products are as good as, if not better than, foreign products, so the Chinese people are happy to use them. Foreign manufacturers cannot produce light bulbs larger than 500 watts in Shanghai and must import them from their home countries. China can produce light bulbs up to 2,000 watts on its own. Furthermore, China's selling price is generally 20% cheaper than foreign brands. Therefore, China is able to defeat foreign products, giving the Chinese a sense of pride. Due to space limitations, other details cannot be fully described.

Sino-French and Sino-Youth Teams Victorious Yesterday; Another Match Sees Hexing B Defeat Guanghua 177

The seventh Sino-Youth Basketball League held its second day of competition yesterday, with a total of five matches. The first two matches were Sino-French vs. Yucai and Sino-Youth vs. Huasheng. Due to the disparity in strength, these matches were one-sided. The third match, Hexing B vs. Guanghua, was more closely contested, with the two teams being evenly matched. The final two matches, Zhongji vs. Qiyi and Guohua vs. Shanghai B, were more exciting. The results of each division are summarized below:

Sino-French Defeats Yucai In recent times, Sino-French's basketball skills have been unusually excellent. They have gradually emerged in the various church school basketball leagues in the past winter. Last night's match against Yucai posed a significant threat to Yucai due to the disparity in strength. Sino-French led 22-11 in the first half. In the second half, Sino-French relaxed slightly and lost 7-9. The final score was 29-20, with Sino-French winning.

Sino-Youth Overcomes Huasheng The second match was Sino-Youth vs. Huasheng, with a clear difference in strength. The Sino-Youth team consists mostly of veteran players, while Huasheng is a young team. Naturally, they were no match. In yesterday's match, Sino-Youth's star player, Chen Xianglong, made bold and decisive moves, unstoppable in his attacks, scoring ten points by himself. The portly Dai Changling ran all over the court, earning himself a full sweat. Xu Daogeng also made seven shots, which was commendable. Sino-Youth led 20-14 in the first half and 46-11 in the second half. The final score was 66-25, with Sino-Youth easily defeating Huasheng.

Hexing Defeats Guanghua The third match was Hexing B vs. Guanghua Optical Company. Both teams are emerging teams, with their skills not yet fully refined and their coordination relatively loose. The strength of both sides was average, and there was no exciting performance in the entire match. The score was very close. Hexing's offense was slightly more intense, while Guanghua was disadvantaged by its smaller players. Hexing B led 10-7 in the first half. Both teams scored 12 points in the second half. The final score was 22-19, with Guanghua being defeated. In terms of individual skills, Zhou Pu and Wu Sanjiang of Hexing were relatively active, and their throws were more accurate. He Yutian of Guanghua was able to attack and defend, and is also a promising talent.
