British Elementary School Physical Education Class Team Training Method (II) 180

— Hu

IV. Team Division Methods

There are four common team division methods:

The first is to divide teams based on the children's abilities.

The second is to divide teams based on the children's interests.

The third is to divide teams based on the children's physical condition.

The fourth is to divide teams based on the nature of the teaching materials.

These four methods can be used interchangeably. Therefore, it may be useful to make slight changes to the team organization to adapt to the needs. Changes in team organization can also help with discipline and enable children to cooperate willingly under the leadership of anyone. Moreover, if the team organization lacks changes for a long time, it can lead to excessive competition between teams. However, to foster loyalty and responsibility among children towards a team, the team organization must also have a certain degree of permanence to produce good results. As for the team's markings, various team colors can be used to indicate them. The team names can also be jointly selected by the children. After the children have selected the team names and team colors, they can adopt a mark to show the distinction. Usually, boys can wear a color-faced and white-bottomed headscarf on their heads. Before the team is divided, the boys in each team can show the white bottom, the whole class is uniformly white. When the team activity is implemented, the boys in each team can show the team-colored side, and each team can be distinguished clearly in a moment, and it is very clear. For girls, a ribbon representing the team color can be tied on the hair, on the one hand, it can tie the hair, for decoration, on the other hand, it can be used for team division.

V. Team Training Method

General principles of team training:

(I) Let the children choose their own leaders and decide on their team names and colors.

(II) Train leaders to speak and give simple commands. Initially, teachers can lead the entire class to say simple commands to enable children to distinguish between strong and weak commands. Later, leaders can practice giving commands and let them find appropriate language to explain what they want to do. Do not allow leaders to explain the leadership method in a whisper.

(III) There is also a vice-leader in the team. The vice-leader is not just a nominal title. Sometimes, when the team needs to be divided into two groups, the vice-leader can lead the other group.

(IV) The team leader must remember that he is also a member of the team. When representing various activities, he must also participate in rotation.

Leader Training

The training of leaders is the core of team training. If teachers want to train each team completely, they must train good leaders in advance. During team activities, the leader is the teacher's representative, responsible for leading the entire team to work together. Teachers should train children to have a certain understanding of the concept of leaders as soon as possible. Teachers should not expect too much from leaders. Some children may not be able to serve as leaders due to a lack of ability. Therefore, teachers do not have to hope that every child can become a good leader. The important principle is that the task of the leader should be assigned to all children in rotation as much as possible.

Training a capable leader requires a considerable period of training. Therefore, each leader should be given sufficient time to show his ability. After a child is elected as a leader, he should show his leadership and command ability. He must also have correct performance ability and skills in other activities. It is of course best if the leader can be a first-class representative, otherwise, he must at least be able to understand the purpose of activities and games, distinguish good and bad performances, and pay attention to whether his companions are following the rules. Teachers should also pay attention not to concentrate all their attention on the leader. Teachers should encourage all members of the team to use common sense to take responsibility for themselves and to assist their partners when necessary.

Little Man 185

Nader had been invited to be a partner before and considered it an honor, so he diligently went north every day to find eggs, kept the accounts clearly, and also increased his income a little because of his efforts.

"Ah, Tao Mo! Do you really have to do this?" he said, feeling that if this happened, his reputation would have no place in the trading market from now on.

"I have to do this," Tao Mo replied firmly. "Aimi said that when someone encroaches on (meaning takes the money out of) the property of a company, another person sues him, or uses other methods to attack him, and is unwilling to have anything to do with him anymore. Now you have encroached on my property; I will neither sue you nor hit you, but I have to dissolve our partnership, because I cannot trust you, and of course I don't want to fail."

"Since I can't make you believe in me, and you are not willing to accept my money, but I would rather give you all my money, as long as you are willing to say that you believe that I took the money, then I am still grateful to you. Please be sure to let me still find eggs for you; I don't want any wages, I just do it for free. I am familiar with all the places where eggs are laid, and I love to do this," Nader pleaded.

But Tao Mo shook his head, and his round and interesting face looked suspicious and cold when he decided and said simply, "No; it's better if you are not familiar with it. Don't secretly go and look for me again, and have any plans on my eggs."

Changes in the Gold Exchange's Method of Collecting Market Accounts

The Gold Exchange has changed its method of collecting market accounts, which has been scheduled to be implemented from the 20th of this month. The method is: regardless of whether the broker is a buyer or a seller, after the transaction is completed, there is no need to first stamp the other party, and then fill in the small market account clearly. Use the return receipt book to hand it over to the market affairs section to verify that there are no errors, and then register the account. It must be handed over as soon as it is done according to the market, and no later than five minutes after the transaction (the duplicate account bottom is kept by the broker for verification). Once the account is verified and registered, it cannot be requested to be cancelled or changed. When the amount of conditions and the price are different for the buyer or the seller, the market affairs section will notify both brokers to accompany the official to correct the error. If both parties shirk responsibility and delay resolution, the market affairs section may cancel it for both parties. If one party has submitted the market account, but the other party has not submitted the market account, the market affairs section will notify the broker who has already submitted the market account to urge the other party to submit it quickly. If the other party still does not submit the small market account after being notified, the market affairs section may cancel the unilateral transaction on the small market account that has already been submitted. The small market accounts submitted by the broker to the market affairs section at the close of the market should be verified by the broker before leaving the office. The price numbers on the small market accounts should be written in detail one by one. In order to be convenient, at least "ten," "yuan," and "jiao" must be written. The small market account paper and the return receipt book are made by the exchange. Each broker can use the folding method to receive it from the exchange. The paper fee is borne by the broker to avoid arbitrary waste.

Shen Bao Literary Weekly

Night 210

— Mo Fu

Night is a magician.

He brings many terrifying illusions and evil spirits, baring their teeth and claws, threatening me. I feel terror and unease. The night is so long. It's really difficult to push him away. Daylight seems like a flash of lightning, and twenty-four hours are completely occupied by darkness. I have a fever, I have insomnia, my spirit is weak, and my head feels like a bomb that could explode at any moment, drowsy and sinking in the clouds. My curved waist has become a bent bow. ——There will never be a time to straighten up! I thought like this as I paced from one corner of the room to the other. I carefully lifted my overly light steps, stepping on the soft, cottony floor.

A fit of coughing forced me to squat down, and my whole body felt like it was splitting apart in pain. Suddenly, I grew countless wings and flew high into the sky——no, it was still that giant hand that hadn't let go of me for three years, grabbing my disheveled hair and lifting me up——could it be that I was about to ascend to heaven? Before this thought could even turn over, I was suddenly struck by some great force, and I woke up, but this time I had turned into a rolling stone that the shepherd spoke of, plummeting from the towering mountain peak into a bottomless abyss. In my heart, I was still wondering if I would hit a reef. Although it was clear that rolling down this ten-thousand-ren precipice would certainly mean death, I wanted to live, and I struggled as much as I could.

…I woke up, but I was lying on the floor, a pile of bloody phlegm staining my clothes. Once I understood what I had just gone through, I trembled.

With bleary eyes, I saw that furry hand again, which for three years had played out countless terrifying and tragic farces in front of me, and would continue to do so until my last, I knew.

The light gradually dimmed, and the last ray of light was swallowed by the darkness, and the entire room was enveloped in a solemn night.

Finally, I struggled onto the bed, facing the window, opening my eyes wide, and panting as I gazed at the azure-colored glass.

"No, I can't stand this pressure"! I whispered resolutely, but where did I get the strength to retain time? After a hard struggle, I turned on the electric light. This was the only thing I could do, the ability to fight against the darkness. The piercing electric light made me unable to open my eyes.

This disease of mine is not suitable for using my brain, the doctor had warned countless times. It's not that I deliberately resisted either. I knew I should rest, I needed to rest, and I tried my best to stop it from working, but the result was worse, as if the brain was a stubborn snake.

"Die! Die a little faster!"

I shouted angrily, with the same feeling as a prisoner speaking to an executioner.

Clawing at the bed, I longed for a minute of rest, my eyes fixedly staring at the ceiling, my mind spinning, and the ceiling was spinning with it. All sorts of illusions began to jump before my eyes as before, both funny and terrible. Sinking into a sleepwalking state, I felt myself soaring, the sky, or sinking into a deep abyss, flying and racing across mountains and ridges… arriving at an unknown place——no, this is hell, where the demons attack me without restraint… I woke up covered in cold sweat, my heart pounding violently in my chest, my lips trembling, and my eyes wide with fear, looking around in a panic… I will never be able to return to peace again! I looked at the table clock placed on the table, it was only a few tens of minutes, and sighed deeply, followed by terrible coughing. Again and again, sometimes it's a demon giving me a knife to the chest, and bright red blood shoots out like a fountain all over the place. Suddenly, the change is not caused by external forces, the blood is vomiting on its own. Suddenly, a pointy-mouthed monster appeared in front of me, bent down and drank all the blood on the ground, and then tightly embraced me with its thick, hairy arms, inserting a tubular mouth into my chest… I fainted from this unbearable pain; sometimes I saw many friends surrounding my corpse and sighing, and I felt how foolish they should be, isn't this worse than living in sin? Sometimes I'm lying in a tomb in the wilderness… but it contains the same meaning.

The last time I woke up, I mistook the dim light for the morning light, and a glimmer of hope was extinguished again.

Night is hell.

The Way Out for New Poetry and the "Hu Shi Style" 211

— Zi Mo

I am very optimistic about new poetry. The recent trends in the poetry world clearly tell us that new poetry has its way out.

In terms of content, it has shifted from personal sentiments to social colors. In terms of form, it has moved from imitating the carving of rhetoric to using creative colloquial language. We cannot but admit this kind of progress in Chinese new poetry. The "Hu Shi style" that evolved from old poetry and lyrics has only left faint traces in the new poetry movement. Even the "Spring Water style" that was obviously influenced by Tagore and Japanese haiku, and the so-called "New Moon style" that was influenced by Western romantic poets and emphasized "beautiful form" a little later, as well as the obscure symbolic and allegorical style imitated from France a few years ago, only occupy dark and distorted corners in today's new poetry world. Like other departments of literature, what we need for new poetry is the singing of the masses, the grasp and exposure of social reality, and the enlightenment of social trends. And the current new poets are also working hard in this direction.

In terms of form, one difference between poetry and novels, dramas, etc. lies in the economy of its language. However, the so-called economy and non-economy are by no means determined by elegance and vulgarity. A new poem that is piled up and carved with many elegant words, beautiful metaphors, allegories, and even allusions, is not necessarily economical if the content is empty. Conversely, if one can use simple and concrete colloquial language to express reality, and make people have very concrete and profound impressions and feelings, then it is economical and successful poetry.

By saying this, I am not advocating that new poetry does not need "beautiful form" or does not need skills. However, just as a woman's beauty does not lie in applying rouge and powder, wearing corsets, and wearing high heels, beautiful form does not come from imitation and carving. The search for the most flexible and concrete means to powerfully express content is where new poetry should strive in terms of skills. To achieve this goal, the dead, elegant words should not be as good as the living spoken language. The works of the new German poet Becher and many new Russian poets provide us with a good example.

The so-called free poetry of the past few years failed, not because of its inelegance, and even less because of its use of spoken language (because it was not really colloquial), but because of its poor content and immature skills. The shortcomings of the current social new poetry are not that it uses colloquial language, but that it does not use colloquial language well. This is partly related to the author's general technical training and familiarity with the spoken language, and the more important reason is the lack of rich experience of the author in the mass life. Yes, poets like the new Russian poets who came from the lower classes of society have not yet been discovered in China, so the hope for the popularization of new poetry cannot be overly extravagant. However, this direction should and can be striven for. In fact, the achievements in the past few years have not been bad.

It is of course very good if new poems can be sung, but being able to be sung is not an indispensable condition for new poetry. The folk song style or the "Feng Yuxiang style" is relatively stronger than the "Spring Water style" or the "New Moon style", partly because it can be sung, and also because they are popularized——describing the masses and being understood by the masses. If we were to learn from old poetry and lyrics in order to achieve the condition of being able to be sung, even if we succeeded, it would not be a success for new poetry. It must be known that content can determine form, but at the same time, form will also affect content. "Old wine in new bottles" is not feasible either theoretically or from the history of poetry development. Using forms derived from old poetry and lyrics to express new content will always reduce its realism or even "harm the meaning with words."

Having acknowledged the points mentioned above, it is very clear whether the so-called "Hu Shi style" is a way out for new poetry, and whether it should be adopted and promoted.

Taking "In Praise of Little Flying" as a representative work of the so-called "Hu Shi style," even if no tune is filled in, the pattern and odor of "Little Order" are still retained between the lines. The reason why the last few lines are too "literary" is really not surprising, because turning somersaults in this kind of old poetry and lyric skeleton will not only not turn out very far, but also naturally follow its way. Not to mention the expression of the leisure class's "leisurely" mood in the content of this poem. It is true that there are many very popular songs and tunes (especially Yuan songs) that are worth learning from. But the so-called learning is not just imitating or drawing from the styles of Yuan songs or Ming and Qing zaju dramas, but to learn their spirit of boldly, flexibly, and accurately using colloquial language to express themselves. One era has its own literary content, and it also has its own literary form. Just as the relatively elegant Kunqu Opera gave way to Peking Opera, the era of the hobbling "Hu Shi style" has long passed. In the eyes of those who are familiar with old poetry and lyrics—that is, what Mr. Bohan called "that part of people who are well-versed in old poetry and lyrics"—new poetry is naturally not only difficult to understand and pronounce, but also not flavorful enough. But this is not the error of the current new poetry's route, but only the error in the pace when walking this route (the shortcomings of new poetry in content and technique mentioned above), and it is also a temporal error in the views of this part of people. It is very obvious that new poetry does not need to go backward for the sake of this part of people. What we hope from new poets is to do their best to enrich the social content of new poetry, and to creatively use colloquial language to express this content, creating new forms. Needless to say, immersing themselves in the life of the masses, increasing their own experience, and learning vivid skills are even more prerequisites for new poets.

At this time, specially putting forward the "Hu Shi style" and considering it as a way out for new poetry will only result in "this road does not lead anywhere."

The Song of the Flower Seller 212

— Da Bao

Has anyone lost their home?

Please come and buy fresh flowers!

—Lilacs are blooming,

Cherry blossoms are blooming,

Magnolias are blooming…

Has anyone lost their home?

Let me present you with the fragrance of flowers!

—People of Europe,

People of Japan,

People of China…

On the Question of New Poetry's Form 213

— Ren Jun

Last November, I published an article "On the Road of New Poetry" in the third issue of this publication, raising objections to Mr. Chen Zizhan's advice to new poets to follow the "Hu Shi style." Following the publication of that article, I saw Mr. Chen Zizhan's "A Brief Discussion on the Hu Shi Style" and Mr. Bo Han's "Recent Poetry Criticism and Poetic Talks," which partially touched on my debate with Mr. Chen, in the sixth and ninth issues of this publication.

In the article "A Brief Discussion on the Hu Shi Style," Mr. Chen vigorously defended his position and made every effort to annotate his previous article. However, there is one difference: in the previous article, Mr. Chen only vaguely advised new poets to follow the "Hu Shi style," while in this one, he clearly stated: "But I do not hope that you will still take the old road of 'A Book of Experiments,'" because Mr. Chen also believes that "the old road has not shaken off the traces of imitating old poetry, it is really like enlarged feet that have been bound too tightly"; on the contrary, he hopes that people will create poems in the style of "Ode to a Flying Insect," because "such poems can be said to be a new road." That is to say, the "Hu Shi style" that Mr. Chen advises people to follow is the "new road" of "Ode to a Flying Insect," not the old road of "A Book of Experiments."

However, the problem lies here.

Now we must ask: can poems like "Ode to a Flying Insect" really be said to be a new road in terms of the "Hu Shi style"? This is really the main key to the problem, and there should be a definite answer. It is definitely not enough to vaguely say "it seems" to be possible or "it seems" impossible. - And if you want to give a definite answer to this question, I think the most practical and reliable way is to compare it with the works in "A Book of Experiments," which even Mr. Chen considers to be an old road, to see what kind of differences there are between it and them, and how much newer it really is than them.

As far as I know, the works collected in "A Book of Experiments" (I am based on the old version), except for a small part that is written in relatively simple classical Chinese (or called "vernacular"), which cannot be regarded as representative works of Hu Shi's attempt to create new poems, old poems and old lyrics (such as "Mid-Autumn Festival," "On the River," "Qinyuan Spring," "Like a Dream"), most of the remaining works can be said to be of the same type as "Ode to a Flying Insect." Now, let's take the poem "On the Lake" as an example:

A firefly on the water,

A firefly in the water,

Side by side,

Gently,

Flying past the edge of our boat.

The two immortals fly closer and closer,

Gradually merging into one.

Look, what is the difference between "Ode to a Flying Insect" and this type of "Hu Shi style"? What is more refreshing about it? Really, if you have the time and interest, you might as well read "Ode to a Flying Insect" and most of the works in "A Book of Experiments" side by side, and you will definitely feel that the "Ode to a Flying Insect" that is considered a "new road" not only does not exceed them by a single point, but also, even though they are all old works by Hu Shi from more than ten years ago, you can also find many expressive methods that are more free, lively, and farther away from old poetry; although, as the author said, they still "have the bloody smell of the era of foot-binding."

Therefore, I think that if Mr. Chen always considers the "Hu Shi style" to be a "new road" and wants to advise people to take it, that is Mr. Chen's personal freedom, and others have no right to interfere; but if he forcibly tries to find some new goods from the old goods stalls selling outdated goods as the basis for his own position, that is unnecessary. In short, let's take a look at Mr. Bo Han's opinion on this issue. (To be continued)

A Hero of the Age 214

Poverty and Observation 215

— Wang Renshu

——Reading Balzac's Critical Notes——

In Marie's book of criticism on Balzac, there is such a passage at the beginning:

In the ingenious preface to "Facino Cane," Balzac reveals the secret of his creation. - He transcended himself and assimilated himself to the diverse life of the world. Look at the following section, which is a confession.

'At that time, I lived in a small street. Readers may not know it, it is called Rue de la Clef. Facing the spring next to the Place de la Bastille, starting from Rue Sainte-Anne and ending at Rue des Fossés-Saint-Victor. The desire for knowledge threw me into a room on the roof of a certain building. I worked hard here at night. During the day, I spent time in the nearby Mazarine Library. I lived a simple life. Content with all the conditions of a monastic life indispensable to workers. No matter how good the weather, there were hardly any days to take a walk on the Boulevard de Breton. Only once, attracted by some kind of passion, I was drawn away from the habit of research and went out. But, even so, isn't it research? I had to observe the customs of the remote streets, the people who lived there, and their characters. They were as dirty as the workers and just as unceremonious. They were not at all wary of their surroundings. I mingled among them, watching them haggling over sales and arguing with each other when they left work. My observation was already intuitive. It went deep into the souls of people. But it did not neglect the external expressions of the body. It can be said that it first tightly grasped the frank part expressed externally, and then immediately broke into its inside. Such observation gave me the ability to live in the lives of those being observed. Just like the Islamic monks who appeared in Arabian Nights, without chanting any spells, they could take away people's flesh and souls, and I merged with those being observed.

'For example, one night, between eleven and twelve o'clock, I ran into an employee and his wife coming out of the Théâtre des Funambules. I remember following them closely from Pont-aux-Choux Street to Boulevard du Temple. At first, the honest couple talked about the plays they had seen. But the topic shifted from one to another, and gradually they talked about their own affairs. The wife never heard the child whining, even though she was pulling the child along. The couple were calculating tomorrow's income, and wanted to use the money in twenty different ways. First, they carefully talked about arranging their livelihood: how the value of potatoes was very high, the winter was getting longer, firewood was becoming more expensive, and about the opinion of borrowing money from the bakery, they all told each other. Their discussions were very enthusiastic, and the different personalities of the two people were indeed very well displayed in their words. Hearing the words of such people, I became a part of their lives. I seemed to feel their tattered clothes on my back. My feet were walking in their shoes with holes. Their desires and hopes all rushed into my soul. Perhaps my soul was already connected to their souls. This is a dream of those who have their eyes open. The boss of the factory abused them, the hooligans, and didn't give them money, running around for nothing. These words made me angry along with them. Abandoning one's own habits, immersing oneself in the intoxication of spiritual action, indulging in such a game, this is my comfort. Who allowed me to have such talent, such insight? This is probably a quality that will eventually be abused. I will never explore the reasons for the origin of such an ability. I only say that I have this ability and can use this ability. From that time on, I began to analyze the various elements of the uneven group under the term "the people." I had to evaluate their good or bad qualities to engage in analyzing the masses. What I want to let readers know is only this. What is the use of remote streets to me? From that time on, I suddenly understood. Remote streets are the training ground for various changes. Here, heroes, inventors, scholars of strength, rascals, extremely evil villains, virtuous people, hooligans, etc., are all oppressed by poverty, panting under persecution, drowning in wine, and exhausting their bodies and minds with strong drinks to bury their lives..."'

Not stopping at the appearance and surface of things, but being able to penetrate into the root of life that determines other things, and becoming a great revealer of the surrounding life, this is the essence of a genius observer. He has the courage to see society in reality, and he can describe this society in fierce attacks. He can break in with the incorruptible beauty of his eyes, and call out the true tasks of the laws and religions that many powers are working hard to advance. From this, he gives an immeasurable gift to those who can recognize the world in which they live. He preaches to those people, and he believes that nothing in the world is not interconnected. Everything contains meaning in itself, but knowing how to distinguish this meaning becomes a problem. He often draws deep and novel lessons for people from various facts. Therefore, among the great teachers of mankind who are advancing towards conscious thought, his position is very high. ..."

This passage, I think, is very useful for people engaged in creation. I have said elsewhere that writers are easily swayed to distort the truth of reality with their subjective opinions. It makes the people who appear in the work seem to be dragged into the story. But as Balzac said, observation as a practice of life is naturally different. Because he is not standing aside and making calm observations, but living in the lives of those being observed. The reason for this, as Marie said elsewhere: "He has a sharp sense of the nature of the times and the conditions that determine it. He discovers the hub of the wheel there." But what cultivates his sharp senses? "He knows the terrifying struggle of society, and in the battle with the world of money, he resolutely formed himself with extremely heavy suffering. This is the reason why his works miraculously become so alive, and this is also the reason why he has the possibility of breaking into the core of the world. Under the constant whip of poverty, he grasps his era fully and intensely."

So what poverty gave Balzac was: it made him tough and brave, and in order to escape the heavy burden that the world hated on him, he ignited the fire of his creation when necessary. But this is also a liberation that transforms his daily suffering into magnificent radiation. He said: "Only when I work can I forget my pain. Work saved me, which is the best explanation. Likewise, due to poverty, he knew the importance of economic conditions in the totality of social life. In his works, we can see that those who cannot adapt to life and the new necessities of the transitional period in the economic structure of society are gradually falling behind. "The whole era, with its pressing reality, passes before his great mirror, allowing people to recognize the rise of the power of the bourgeoisie in that era, which arose along with the powerful development of industry and commerce, the movement of the aristocracy towards the victorious bourgeoisie, the overthrow of the old forms of life, and the establishment of new classes that brought out their own forms of life in all fields...etc."

Here, we can also say: remote streets are the training ground for various changes. And the life of poverty is the whip that encourages genius to exert its greatest talent. He not only understands the truth of this society in suffering, but also makes magnificent internal radiation in suffering. Uniting the necessity required by the heart with the necessity from an objective point of view, this becomes the reason for Balzac's greatness.

Whistle 216

— Long Gonggong

When I was very young, I received different warnings from my father and mother. My father heard me whistling, stared at me sternly, and said that it was a lowly behavior. My mother did not forbid me during the day, but when she heard me pursing my lips and making that sharp sound at night, she said to me in a terrified, pleading way:

"Don't make this strange noise, don't, it will attract ghosts."

But in some later experiences, I really liked that natural flute that some people thought would attract demons. Its sound is not a strange noise, it is the breath of human emotion, clear, beautiful, and different from any musical instrument - no musical instrument can be compared. The sound of human voice cannot be imitated.

Those things happened in different places. One time it was in the morning, and I was walking on a country path with a young farmer who was short and very alert. I heard him whistling, like a lonely mountain song, or a happy pastoral song. I saw a pure, lively, and kind person. I was proud to have such a human being walking with me. On a sea ship, I heard someone whistling a low tune; there was no sea, no clouds in front of me, (although they were so great and lovely) I lost my own place, and almost thought - or even saw - my two friends without any illusion: young, brave, and loving the truth, one was far away in some place, and the other had died without any regrets. If I had not discovered this same song, I would have thought that no one else understood this song. Another time, on a small, winding mountain, in order to find someone who was already good and didn't know where he was hiding, I whistled the short song that we both liked, and suddenly, I found the familiar sound.

I can now judge a person's ideals, character, and habits from the whistle he blows. At first, I thought it was my own absurdity, or at most just a coincidence.

Some people whistle badly, very brokenly, or blow vulgar tunes, or make sounds without scales, or simply don't know what they are whistling.

I know some blacksmiths, when their emotions suddenly relax, they will whistle a long whistle. Sometimes on the road, you can hear some free tunes created by coolies mixed with humming. Next to the university, it's not surprising, anyone will hear some smug popular movie songs.

My observation of people proves my own clumsiness. I can never infer whether a person is good or bad from his words, face, bones, or way of dealing with people. Even if I know he has done something stupid, I still can't decide his category. - So I have to rely on other methods.

If he can whistle, I hope he will whistle for me to hear. I whistle first, thinking:

"The mouth is not only for eating and speaking. You won't lose its value if you use it to do other better things."

My greatest disappointment is if he remains silent at this time.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

The Activity of Military Alliances 217

— Xing An

Regardless of whether the Second World War will break out this year, it is obvious that 1936 is a very serious period. The Italian and Ethiopian armies are still deadlocked, which is one of the crises. The London Naval Conference is on the verge of collapse, which has a considerable impact on the future of the situation. Also, in East Asia, on the one hand, imperialism is intensifying its attack on our country, and on the other hand, there is the opposition between Japan and Russia, which is enough to threaten world peace. What is particularly disturbing is that various news about military alliances has been spreading from various places recently. The smell of gunpowder has permeated the world, and this year is the most dangerous day when a great disaster is imminent!

There are a total of four rumors about military alliances: one is the Japanese-German alliance, the second is the Soviet-Russian alliance with Outer Mongolia, the third is the Sino-Japanese alliance, and the fourth is the British-Japanese alliance. Some of these news are naturally very unreliable and can only be regarded as a propaganda effect on a certain aspect, but some are quite convincing. For example, the Japanese-German alliance has been widely rumored by all parties, and it has been rumored repeatedly for a year. Now there are even rumors that they secretly signed a military alliance agreement four months ago. Although this matter cannot be verified and has been denied by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, it is said that the Japanese-German alliance was negotiated by the Japanese military attache stationed in Berlin and the German defense representatives. It is said that the Japanese military department changed its approach and took direct action in order to avoid the Ministry of Foreign Affairs from coming forward.

The Japanese-German military alliance is not only widely rumored by all parties, but also very possible from the perspective of facts. The two countries have shown several similar characteristics. Japan is a militaristic country, and Germany is also a militaristic country. They are both traitors to the League of Nations, both tearers of treaties, both have the ambition to seize colonies, and both have enemies with conflicting interests (Japan's enemy is the United States, and Germany's enemy is France). Also, the two countries have the same stance in opposing Soviet Russia. According to some rumors, this time the Japanese-German alliance has two goals: one is a military secret agreement, and the other is a public agreement against communism. In this way, their collusion is nothing more than carrying out their atrocities of destroying world peace and encroaching on the weak under the cover of the anti-Russian banner!

The alliance between Soviet Russia and Outer Mongolia is also possible from the perspective of the two countries' opposition to Japan. The conflict between Japan and Russia has become increasingly acute. The situation during the recent disputes between the two countries is very dangerous. Some people speculate that a Japanese-Russian war is inevitable. As for Japan and Outer Mongolia, the threat of the Japanese puppet army to Outer Mongolia has become more urgent recently. The Outer Mongolian authorities have reportedly made up their minds to prepare to resist. It can be seen that their opposition to Japan is consistent. The visit of the Outer Mongolian Prime Minister and his party to Soviet Russia certainly has some political implications. However, this news about the military alliance between Soviet Russia and Outer Mongolia is only seen in Japanese propaganda, and it is not known whether it has other effects. However, judging from the policy recently adopted by Soviet Russia in diplomacy (i.e., peaceful diplomacy), it is unlikely that a military alliance will be concluded.

As for the Sino-Japanese alliance, it was advocated by Japan's Hirota. China and Japan jointly requested the Soviet Russian government to open up Outer Mongolia. If rejected, China and Japan would form a military alliance to deal with it. Regarding this matter, it was originally a big question whether China and Japan had the possibility of concluding an alliance.

The British-Japanese military alliance is a restoration of the old alliance, and the possibility is also very high. Before the European War, Britain and Japan concluded an alliance. Recently, people from both sides have repeatedly brought it up again. This was advocated by a part of the British naval community, believing that since the United States is mired in an isolationist policy and has failed to intervene in Far Eastern affairs, China and Japan can form a general understanding. If the British-Japanese alliance can be restored, Britain's interests in China can be maintained. Not long ago, it was widely rumored that Britain and the United States would jointly confront Japan, but now there is news of a British-Japanese alliance. International relations are so complicated. However, a look at Britain's recent accommodation to Japan in the naval conference shows that the rumors are not entirely unfounded. In order to maintain its position in the Far East, Britain hopes to restore its alliance with Japan.

The activity of military alliances is a harbinger of the coming of war!

Winter News 218

— Luo Zhihua

The streets are desolate and quiet. The once bustling pedestrians have all shrunk into woolen garments.

Walking on this deserted street, I feel like I'm stepping into a dilapidated courtyard, and my heart feels a little desolate. Looking at the upright French parasol trees, I think of the distant northern lands, the people of the northern lands, and the rustling white poplars of the northern lands.

The south is filled with warmth, drifting with the fragrant scent of warm flowers and the cries of crows. Today, however, it has turned into a piercing cold.

In the past, I was a dreamer. The South in my dreams was draped in the azure blue of spring all year round: whether in the countryside or in the city, it was bathed in the warm breeze of March. Of course, this dream is shattered. Like any corner of the world (except for that one-sixth of the land), it is plagued by hunger and cold. It is like a syphilitic patron, entertaining and struggling frantically. It knows its future very clearly. When I set foot on the land of the South, stepping onto the asphalt roads of Shanghai, what follows is this familiar demon: hunger and cold.

In summer or spring, I worry about the arrival of winter. I am afraid to see it, its stern face.

But it has come after all, sweeping away the leaves, sweeping away the green of the fields, and even sweeping away the warmth of people's bodies: the whole world is trapped in an ice cellar.

Stepping on the bright and solid asphalt road, a chill rises from the soles of my feet. My heart feels it quickly, my lips chatter, my fingers ache and feel cold, as if they have been taken out from a tight squeeze. The sharp northwest wind, carrying an unresolvable anger, freezes my nose red and drills into my thin, loose sleeves! Everything is winter: the winter streets, the winter wind, me, a winter pedestrian.

Winter is cold, cruel, and forever cursed. Of course, I cannot praise winter as I would praise spring. However, when a person is driven mad by passion, they need a bit of the winter wind to wake them up. Just as a person is born in the spring of youth, the spring breeze gives them the power to grow, gives them the love to grow, and they grow. When the summer-like middle age arrives, they scatter the seeds of life like a storm, attacking their enemies like madmen. They have no thoughts, no worries. However, when the autumn-like old age arrives, everything withers and declines with the blowing of the autumn wind. Although the flame of youth has not completely extinguished, people in their forties are full of fiery complaints. Now, in this kind of winter, people are old. They caress the palms of their hands, polished by the grind of life, and with a mind that is calmer than ice, they count the wrinkles on their foreheads, blowing the experiences, those fallen-leaf-like experiences, into the mud with the wind, to be used as a reference for their children who come after them.

Winter is cold, clearing away the heart enveloped by passionate love threads.

In the embrace of winter, we review the memories of the year. That way, we can decide how to start our steps next year. We will use all our strength to unleash the power that the spring season gives us, towards the road of life.

I am still stepping on that cold asphalt road. It presents a shining black iron face, just like the face of life.

However, even if the sound of my chattering teeth is louder, even if the wind blows harder, I have no time to care. I walk forward.

Turning the corner, it is a busier road. The streetcar, with its urgent shouts, flies by as if escaping the pursuit of winter. People's heads are shrunk into their overcoat collars, and their hands are hidden in animal fur. They are escaping winter, just like an old man fearing the approach of death.

Passing this street, it returns to the desolate road. I listen to the rhythm of my footsteps, the sound of the streetcar that has already gone far away, and my eyes look at the swirling tung leaves. My heart is filled with desolation, especially when I think of the people of the North and the rustling white poplars of the North.

Walking on the road, in the winter wind.

Window 219

— Simon

For it, the window, I have many memories and feelings.

Once a person hides in a house, although they may not suddenly feel detached from the world, they are at least temporarily separated from the chaotic things outside. And it, the window, seems to be a bridge, connecting your heart to everything outside the window. Looking down from the window, there may be a chaotic street scene, the noisy sounds of people and vehicles pouring into your ears, immediately making you restless again. Therefore, the direction of the window is best if it does not face the street. Looking down, there is only a lonely and quiet alley, and it is not easy to hear the sound of people's footsteps for a long time. And looking up: it is the tip of a house covered in the lush green shade of tall hazel trees, red, blue, brilliantly shining in the bright sunlight. The sky is clear, light blue, without a single cloud, like an uncolored painting. And occasionally, a little bit of soaring wings appear from the distant sky, as if written into the distance.

A very relaxed and pleasant mood surges into my heart.

That pleasantness, that ease, comes from the window. If the direction of the window is changed to face the street, you will hate and curse it for no reason, and then angrily close the window.

Find a house with a window that has beautiful scenery outside. In the long days, in different seasons, the proper window location of a house is indeed very important and necessary. Because of it, the relationship of the window often transforms a person's state of mind. In the hot summer, a south-facing window still has a cool breeze blowing in from time to time in the hot air, allowing you to take a breath. If it is a west-facing window, the poisonous sun of June fills the room, and people simply become wontons in a steamer. Once, for a year in the summer, I was annoyed for some time because of a west-facing window. Moving to another house in an instant was impossible, so the house was like a burning pit, and I spent a summer that felt like half a century. By the time autumn came, I had been ground down until I didn't look much like a person anymore. Even now, thinking about it, I still hate it a little, that west-facing window.

When the harsh winter comes, the window must not face north. However, in winter, even if there are several windows, they do not face north, but are always tightly closed and not often opened. Moreover, a stove has been lit in the house. Through a window, separated from the world, I have not forgotten the world at the same time, only blocking it with a layer of glass. Looking out the window, the earth is desolate, and there is no excellent scenery. The branches of the ruined trees tremble in the dark sky.

At this time, the window has less leisurely interest for you and more gloomy feelings. Because there is a dim sky outside the window, because of the misty dusk under the sway of wind and rain, because another year is approaching its end, you will inevitably have a slight, smoky thought. Towards the hazy window outside, where small snowflakes are falling, your thoughts suddenly become unusually heavy.

In the night, it is silent, only letting the wind shake the window, the glass frame rattling, breaking through the still air in the room. Besides this, there is no other sound. And a person listens intently. The sound waves, sometimes heavy and sometimes light, cause one's thoughts to rise and fall like the tide. This disturbance will keep you tossing and turning until late at night, unable to sleep, even enduring until dawn in a pile of desolate and unbearable illusions. It, the window hit by the wind, often has times that make you suffer like this. But you cannot lack a window after all. When dawn breaks, a faint ray of light shines through the window, telling you that it is morning. When dusk comes, the light on the window gradually dims, you glance outside, and the thick haze embraces the earth, and you know that night has come.

The house I am currently living in does not even have a window with the worst direction. When I raise my eyes, my sight is blocked by wooden boards on all sides. It is like being hidden in a dark cellar, losing the window's revelation of time, and completely unaware of how the day begins and when it gets dark. This life is like groping in the eternal night, making me eagerly pursue even a window with an extremely bad direction.

Page 18

School Dismissal 220

— Bai Xi

It is time for school dismissal again. The principal of XX Private Elementary School, Le Sitong, has a thousand knots in his stomach and is so anxious that his eyes are red! He finally managed to get through a semester. In this semester, he was actually able to live through it; it is a truth he can't understand no matter how hard he tries.

Everyone has self-esteem, especially the young Principal Le Sitong. But for this elementary school, no, for being unwilling to leave the innocent and pure children, he has endured the insults and scolding of the creditors. He, shamelessly, humbly, even almost kneeling, speaks kindly to the creditors... Heaven! I can't think about everything anymore! Let the past be the past! How to deal with the immediate difficulties?

At present: he is busy with the semester exams, but through these semester exams, isn't his miserable fate nakedly revealed? Recently, he has been particularly good to the young students. Even if they have a little bit of rule-breaking behavior, he advises them kindly, not like he used to use a stern attitude to severely reprimand them. Why is this? Isn't it because the semester is about to end, and he is deeply afraid that they will switch schools?

Every time a young student has been kindly advised by him, he regrets it and hates himself. Why am I making such a lowly action? Am I not a mentor to the children? If children make mistakes, they must be severely reprimanded! Yes, I have insulted the children's personality! I am treating the children as commodities! Alas! Ah!...

Le Sitong, this young principal, hangs his head to his chest. He really wants to cry his heart out. But he suddenly thinks: hasn't he often heard a burst of whispering gossip among the elementary school students recently?

"Hey! XX school's tuition is two yuan!"

"Ours here is five yuan!"

"Too expensive!"

The world has indeed progressed a lot! The concepts of "expensive" and "cheap" have been clearly understood by the children! Alas! A new elementary school has opened in the alley next door, charging only two yuan for tuition. Look! Recruitment advertisements are plastered all over the alleys. The four words "two yuan tuition" are so striking! Not counting the big advertisements, they also go door-to-door to distribute flyers, saying things like: "This school, in view of the recent economic downturn," "This school, in order to promote universal education, charges only two yuan for tuition," and so on, pulling on a big pile. Heaven! Nowadays, parents find it difficult to earn money. Who wouldn't want to send their children to an elementary school with low fees?... But in this way, Principal Le Sitong is worried to death!

In addition to the blow of "two yuan tuition," Principal Le Sitong is also suffering from the blow of the "Notice to Parents" flyer. The content of the flyer says: Schools that are not registered are unreliable. Often, people falsely use the name of running a school, collect a bunch of tuition fees, and "run away." Therefore, please do not send your children to study at schools that have not been registered... Of course, this negative article is to tell people to send their children to registered schools!... But in this way, Principal Le Sitong is even more worried to death!

Looking at the group of elementary school students in front of him, Principal Le Sitong's head is dizzy! To the left of his school alley is a newly opened school that only charges "two yuan tuition," and to the right is a registered school!... Heaven!

He hates himself for accommodating the students, but he has to accommodate the students. He hates himself for promoting to the students like a merchant, saying: "Our school teaches well," but he has to promote to the students like a merchant, saying: "Our school teaches well"! He hates himself, even hates his wife, children, father, mother, and, by extension, he hates his children. Without them, wouldn't he not have to say those words?

But he still has to live... He is wrong! He mocks his lack of awareness. But he hates himself even more because he is cowardly.

The time for school dismissal is approaching day by day.

Broadcasting

Ballad Singing 221

Xia Hesheng, Three Smiles

Dunben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening Chapter "Dream of the Red Chamber, Daiyu's Return to Heaven"

The deafening drums and music are as noisy as the tide. In the Grand View Garden, there are many voices. It turns out that, Brother Bao is getting married tonight. Servants are running back and forth, each on their own errands. Little do they know that Lin Daiyu, in Xiaoxiang Pavilion, is terminally ill and emaciated. Only Zijuan and Xueyan are loyally serving her. No one visits, and she is doubly lonely. The girl, her liver fire is rising, her cheeks are red, and her whole body is in pain, difficult to describe. Her breath is as fine as a gossamer, on the verge of death. Zijuan is so anxious that her limbs are weak, and her heartstrings seem to be burning with fierce fire. She thinks of Mother Li, who is usually a good person. She orders a little maid to invite her from Daoxiang Village. Li Wan, hearing this, gets up and comes to visit with great concern. Seeing her, her teeth are clenched and difficult to open, her eyes are slightly open and her lips are moving slightly. Her mind is unclear and she is dizzy for a long time. Zijuan and Li Wan cry sadly. As the sun sets in the west and the bright moon shines, a lamp is as small as a bean, and the bamboo sways in the wind. The girl's illness has slightly recovered, and she opens her eyes to look. She can drink the tea and beckons with her hand. She says to Zijuan, "My friendship with you is as close as hands and feet, and I call you my confidante. I have something important to ask you to do. I am as flawless as white jade. Tell them to send me home for a visit." Saying this, her breath becomes rapid, her hands and feet are as cold as ice, and she is covered in cold sweat. The pupils in her eyes have lost their light, and her fists are clenched tightly. Zijuan's tears have been flowing non-stop. Her heart is cut like a knife, and she cries sadly. Li Wan and Tanchun also arrive. Hearing her, she repeatedly uses her strength to call out "Bao Yu." Alas, as soon as she says "Goodbye," she returns to heaven. In an instant, the jade is lost and the fragrance is gone. She returns to the Land of Sorrow to become an immortal.

Du Wenkui, Zhou Jianhong, Red Robe

Sino-Western (1040) 12:15 AM to 1:00 AM

Opening Chapter "Gold and Beauty"

What in the world easily moves the heart? I fear it is gold and beauty. Gold can take away a commoner's will. A beauty's words are like an imperial edict. Look at the many young people who are suffering setbacks, also for gold and beauty. Remember that Xiang Yu, the hero of Chu, committed suicide at Wujiang. He was reluctant to part with his beautiful Yu. Look at the corrupt officials who compete for power. They are constantly thinking about gold. Some are fighting with their brothers over gold. Some are harming others for wealth. Some are making enemies of their loved ones for gold. Some are separating husband and wife for gold. Some are losing their conscience in an instant for gold. Some are losing their integrity and bodies for gold. Gold, I think you are an evil spirit with supreme power. I don't know how many people you have harmed. I see you turning black and white upside down with great power. So it is that gold can buy a beauty's heart. Look at the beauties of ancient times, who have great magical power, not only overturning the country but also overturning the city. Remember that in the Romance of the Three Smiles, Tang Jieyuan was affectionate for a beauty. In the Double Pearl Phoenix, Wen Bizheng sold his body and relied on the heavenly official's door. He didn't want to be a scholar, but was willing to be a lowly person. Don't laugh, don't look down on him. What's wrong with being fond of beauty and loving beauties? Beauty, I hate you for bullying others with your power. I hate you for only valuing clothes and not valuing people. Because of you, compatriots have differences of opinion. Because of you, fathers and sons actually quarrel. I think, if there were no gold in the world, thieves would not be rampant. If there were no gold in the world, countries could not only be strong but also be healthy. If there were no gold in the world, why snatch inheritances and harm lives? If there were no gold in the world, good families would not revolt. All because of the glittering gold that dazzles people's eyes. All because of the beauty that stirs up greed. Look at the men who are greedy for lust in nineteen out of ten cases, and the women who have always loved gold and silver. Therefore, gold and silver are in love with each other. For whom do so many heroes die? As countless as the sands of the Ganges, they die for these two things. They act as tyrants and play with people.

Film

"Love Letter" Renamed "Peach and Plum Contending for Beauty" 224

"Love Letter," written and directed by Li Pingqian, starring Ye Qiuxin, Gu Lanjun, Wang Zhengxin, Sun Min, etc., is an all-dialogue singing sound film, depicting the suffering of young men and women, love disputes, and reflecting the social economic downturn, pointing out the proper way out for young people. Li Pingqian's previous directorial works have always been known for their delicate style. In order to make the title more in line with the content of the story, "Love Letter" has now been renamed "Peach and Plum Contending for Beauty." Judging from this title, it is not difficult to imagine how wonderful and erotic the play is. It is said that the name "Peach and Plum Contending for Beauty" has been approved by the Central Film Inspection Committee.

"Thunder and Lightning Drama Society" Established 225

"Thunder and Lightning Drama Society," with the support of many playwrights, filmmakers, and writers, has been announced. The host is Chen Yi and others.

Their purpose is, of course, to do some dramatic movement on the stage in 1936.

After the establishment of the "Thunder and Lightning Drama Society," the first step is to rehearse plays. The instructors are also well-known figures in the drama and film circles. The internal organization is very strict. They are preparing with considerable expectations to cultivate this newly emerging bud.

Recent News from Yiguang Society 226

Since its establishment, Yiguang Society has been actively rehearsing at all times. All groups are ready, and the first play to be performed will be Yuan Muzhi's "Traitor" and George Bernard Shaw's "Pygmalion."

MGM's Literary Masterpiece "The Good Earth" 227

— Nanjing Today Silent Screening

"Romance in Old Age" 228

—In "After the Calamity, Peach Blossoms"—

Probably about a month ago, an old couple came to the Star Photography Studio to see the filming of "After the Calamity, Peach Blossoms." Hao Tian photographed Xu Xinyuan and his old lady (played by Shu Xiuwen). Before the outbreak of the Qingdao war, the couple said goodbye. Shu Xiuwen got up and closed the window, turned around and sat on the big sofa, and gently called Xu Xinyuan: "Come, sit here with me!" So the two of them sat together intimately. Shu Xiuwen stared at him blankly, as if she had a lot to say in her heart. Suddenly, she laughed to herself, reached out and took Xu Xinyuan's hand and said: "Actually, I don't have anything to say to you. We have been talking for more than thirty years. We have said a lot. Come and sit closer to me, take my hand, let's just sit like this for a while!"

The old couple sat hand in hand silently, like young lovers. This scene is moving and interesting. Mr. Lao She has a short story called "Romance in Old Age" - this "Romance in Old Age" scene, seen by an old couple watching the filming next to them, felt so familiar and laughed at each other.
